        // =================================================================
        // APPLICATION STATE
        // =================================================================
        
        const APP_STATE = {
            currentSectionIndex: 0,
            currentLanguage: 'en', // Changed default to English
            answers: {},
            encryptionKeyConfigured: false
        };

        // =================================================================
        // ENCRYPTION CONFIGURATION
        // =================================================================
        
        // Test encryption key (exactly 32 characters for AES-256)
        const TEST_ENCRYPTION_KEY = "MyTestKey12345678901234567890"; // 32 chars for testing

        /**
         * Setup encryption key - prompts user for master password on first use
         */
        async function setupEncryptionKey(retryCount = 0) {
            const MAX_RETRIES = 3;
            
            if (retryCount >= MAX_RETRIES) {
                alert('Maximum number of attempts exceeded. Please reload the page.');
                throw new Error('Max password attempts exceeded');
            }
            
            let storedKeyHash = localStorage.getItem('encryption_key_hash');
            
            if (! storedKeyHash) {
                // First time setup:  Use test key for development
                const useTestKey = confirm(
                    'DEVELOPMENT MODE\n\n' +
                    'Do you want to use the test encryption key?\n' +
                    '(For production, click "Cancel" to set a custom password)'
                );
                
                let adminKey;
                if (useTestKey) {
                    adminKey = TEST_ENCRYPTION_KEY;
                } else {
                    adminKey = prompt(
                        'IMPORTANT: First-time setup\n\n' +
                        'Please enter a secure master password (min.  16 characters).\n' +
                        'WARNING: If you forget this password, all data will be permanently lost!'
                    );
                    
                    if (!adminKey || adminKey.length < 16) {
                        alert('Password must be at least 16 characters long! ');
                        return setupEncryptionKey(retryCount + 1);
                    }
                }
                
                const keyHash = await crypto.subtle.digest(
                    'SHA-256',
                    new TextEncoder().encode(adminKey)
                );
                const keyHashHex = Array.from(new Uint8Array(keyHash))
                    .map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2, '0'))
                    .join('');
                
                localStorage.setItem('encryption_key_hash', keyHashHex);
                sessionStorage.setItem('derived_key', adminKey);
                
                alert('✅ Master password successfully set! ');
                APP_STATE.encryptionKeyConfigured = true;
                return true;
            } else {
                if (! sessionStorage.getItem('derived_key')) {
                    const enteredKey = prompt('Please enter your master password:');
                    
                    if (!enteredKey) {
                        alert('❌ Password required! ');
                        return setupEncryptionKey(retryCount + 1);
                    }
                    
                    const enteredHash = await crypto.subtle.digest(
                        'SHA-256',
                        new TextEncoder().encode(enteredKey)
                    );
                    const enteredHashHex = Array.from(new Uint8Array(enteredHash))
                        .map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2, '0'))
                        .join('');
                    
                    if (enteredHashHex !== storedKeyHash) {
                        alert('❌ Incorrect password!');
                        return setupEncryptionKey(retryCount + 1);
                    }
                    
                    sessionStorage.setItem('derived_key', enteredKey);
                }
                APP_STATE.encryptionKeyConfigured = true;
                return true;
            }
        }

        /**
         * Derive encryption key from password using PBKDF2
         */
        async function deriveKeyFromPassword(password, salt) {
            const encoder = new TextEncoder();
            const keyMaterial = await crypto.subtle.importKey(
                'raw',
                encoder.encode(password),
                'PBKDF2',
                false,
                ['deriveBits', 'deriveKey']
            );

            return crypto.subtle.deriveKey(
                {
                    name: 'PBKDF2',
                    salt:  salt,
                    iterations: 100000,
                    hash: 'SHA-256'
                },
                keyMaterial,
                { name: 'AES-GCM', length: 256 },
                false,
                ['encrypt', 'decrypt']
            );
        }

        /**
         * Encrypt data with AES-256-GCM
         */
        async function encryptData(data) {
            try {
                const userKey = sessionStorage.getItem('derived_key');
                if (!userKey) {
                    throw new Error('No encryption key available.  Please enter master password.');
                }
                
                const encoder = new TextEncoder();
                const salt = crypto.getRandomValues(new Uint8Array(16));
                const iv = crypto.getRandomValues(new Uint8Array(12));
                
                const key = await deriveKeyFromPassword(userKey, salt);
                
                const encryptedData = await crypto.subtle.encrypt(
                    {
                        name: 'AES-GCM',
                        iv: iv
                    },
                    key,
                    encoder.encode(data)
                );

                const result = new Uint8Array(salt.length + iv.length + encryptedData.byteLength);
                result.set(salt, 0);
                result.set(iv, salt.length);
                result.set(new Uint8Array(encryptedData), salt.length + iv.length);

                const base64 = btoa(result.reduce((data, byte) => data + String.fromCharCode(byte), ''));
                return base64;
            } catch (e) {
                console.error("Encryption error:", e);
                throw new Error("Encryption failed:  " + e.message);
            }
        }

        /**
         * Decrypt data with AES-256-GCM
         */
        async function decryptData(encryptedBase64) {
            try {
                const userKey = sessionStorage.getItem('derived_key');
                if (! userKey) {
                    throw new Error('No encryption key available.  Please enter master password.');
                }
                
                const decoder = new TextDecoder();
                
                const binaryString = atob(encryptedBase64);
                const encryptedArray = new Uint8Array(binaryString.length);
                for (let i = 0; i < binaryString.length; i++) {
                    encryptedArray[i] = binaryString.charCodeAt(i);
                }

                const salt = encryptedArray.slice(0, 16);
                const iv = encryptedArray.slice(16, 28);
                const data = encryptedArray.slice(28);

                const key = await deriveKeyFromPassword(userKey, salt);

                const decryptedData = await crypto.subtle. decrypt(
                    {
                        name: 'AES-GCM',
                        iv: iv
                    },
                    key,
                    data
                );

                return decoder.decode(decryptedData);
            } catch (e) {
                console.error("Decryption error:", e);
                throw new Error("Decryption failed - incorrect password or corrupted data");
            }
        }

        // =================================================================
        // VALIDATION FUNCTIONS
        // =================================================================
        
        /**
         * Validate a single input field
         */
        function validateField(question, value) {
            const errors = [];
            
            // Required check
            if (question.required && (! value || value === '' || (Array.isArray(value) && value.length === 0))) {
                errors.push(getTranslation('validation_required'));
            }
            
            // Skip other validations if empty and not required
            if (! value || value === '') {
                return errors;
            }
            
            // Validation rules
            if (question.validation) {
                const { minLength, pattern } = question.validation;
                
                // Min length
                if (minLength && value. length < minLength) {
                    errors.push(getTranslation('validation_min_length').replace('{min}', minLength));
                }
                
                // Pattern (regex)
                if (pattern) {
                    const regex = new RegExp(pattern);
                    if (!regex.test(value)) {
                        errors.push(getTranslation('validation_pattern'));
                    }
                }
            }
            
            return errors;
        }

        /**
         * Show validation error for a field
         */
        function showFieldError(fieldId, errors) {
            const input = document.getElementById(fieldId);
            const errorElement = document.getElementById(`${fieldId}-error`);
            
            if (input && errors.length > 0) {
                input.classList.add('error');
                if (errorElement) {
                    errorElement.textContent = errors[0];
                    errorElement. classList.add('visible');
                }
                return false;
            } else if (input) {
                input. classList.remove('error');
                if (errorElement) {
                    errorElement.classList.remove('visible');
                }
                return true;
            }
            return true;
        }

        /**
         * Validate all visible fields in current section
         */
        function validateCurrentSection() {
            const section = APP_DATA.sections[APP_STATE.currentSectionIndex];
            let allValid = true;
            
            section.questions.forEach(question => {
                // Skip hidden questions
                if (! checkCondition(question)) {
                    return;
                }
                
                const value = APP_STATE.answers[question.id];
                const errors = validateField(question, value);
                
                if (! showFieldError(question.id, errors)) {
                    allValid = false;
                }
            });
            
            return allValid;
        }

        // =================================================================
        // UTILITY FUNCTIONS
        // =================================================================
        
        /**
         * Get translation for a key
         */
        function getTranslation(key) {
            const lang = APP_STATE.currentLanguage;
            const trans = APP_DATA.translations[lang];
            const labelKey = `label_${key}`;
            return trans? .[labelKey] || trans? .[key] || key;
        }

        /**
         * Sanitize user input to prevent XSS
         */
        function sanitizeInput(input) {
            if (typeof input === 'string') {
                return input
                    .replace(/</g, '&lt;')
                    .replace(/>/g, '&gt;')
                    .replace(/"/g, '&quot;')
                    .replace(/'/g, '&#x27;')
                    .replace(/\//g, '&#x2F;');
            }
            return input;
        }

        /**
         * Check if a question's condition is met
         */
        function checkCondition(item) {
            if (!item.condition) {
                return true;
            }

            const { field, value, operator = '==' } = item. condition;
            const answer = APP_STATE.answers[field];

            if (answer === undefined || answer === null || answer === '') {
                return false;
            }

            if (Array.isArray(answer)) {
                if (operator === 'includes') {
                    return answer. includes(value);
                }
                return false;
            }

            switch (operator) {
                case '==':
                    return answer == value;
                case '!=': 
                    return answer != value;
                case '>':
                    return parseFloat(answer) > parseFloat(value);
                case '<': 
                    return parseFloat(answer) < parseFloat(value);
                case '>=':
                    return parseFloat(answer) >= parseFloat(value);
                case '<=':
                    return parseFloat(answer) <= parseFloat(value);
                default:
                    return false;
            }
        }

        // =================================================================
        // RENDERING FUNCTIONS
        // =================================================================
        
        /**
         * Create date select fields for birth date
         */
        function createDateSelect(question) {
            const wrapper = document.createElement('div');
            wrapper.className = 'date-select-wrapper';
            
            const currentYear = new Date().getFullYear();
            const isLeap = (year) => (year % 4 === 0 && year % 100 !== 0) || year % 400 === 0;

            const createSelect = (id, options, placeholder) => {
                const select = document.createElement('select');
                select.id = id;
                select.name = id;
                select.required = question.required;
                
                const defaultOption = document.createElement('option');
                defaultOption.value = '';
                defaultOption.textContent = placeholder;
                select.appendChild(defaultOption);

                options.forEach(opt => {
                    const option = document.createElement('option');
                    option.value = opt. value;
                    option.textContent = opt.label;
                    select.appendChild(option);
                });
                
                select.value = APP_STATE.answers[id] || '';
                
                select.addEventListener('change', () => {
                    handleAnswerChange(select. id, select.value);
                    
                    // Update days based on month/year
                    if (select.id === '0003_monat' || select.id === '0003_jahr') {
                        const daySelect = document.getElementById('0003_tag');
                        const month = parseInt(document.getElementById('0003_monat').value);
                        const year = parseInt(document.getElementById('0003_jahr').value);
                        
                        if (daySelect && month && year) {
                            let daysInMonth = 31;
                            if ([4, 6, 9, 11].includes(month)) daysInMonth = 30;
                            if (month === 2) daysInMonth = isLeap(year) ? 29 : 28;
                            
                            const currentDay = parseInt(daySelect.value);
                            daySelect.innerHTML = '';
                            
                            const dayDefaultOption = document.createElement('option');
                            dayDefaultOption.value = '';
                            dayDefaultOption.textContent = getTranslation('0003_tag');
                            daySelect.appendChild(dayDefaultOption);

                            for (let i = 1; i <= daysInMonth; i++) {
                                const option = document.createElement('option');
                                option.value = String(i);
                                option. textContent = String(i);
                                daySelect.appendChild(option);
                            }
                            
                            if (currentDay && currentDay <= daysInMonth) {
                                daySelect.value = String(currentDay);
                            } else {
                                daySelect. value = '';
                                handleAnswerChange(daySelect.id, '');
                            }
                        }
                    }
                });

                // Add error message element
                const errorMsg = document.createElement('div');
                errorMsg.className = 'error-message';
                errorMsg.id = `${id}-error`;
                
                const container = document.createElement('div');
                container.appendChild(select);
                container.appendChild(errorMsg);
                
                return container;
            };

            const dayOptions = Array.from({ length: 31 }, (_, i) => ({ value: String(i + 1), label: String(i + 1) }));
            const monthOptions = Array.from({ length: 12 }, (_, i) => ({ value: String(i + 1), label: String(i + 1) }));
            const yearOptions = Array.from({ length: 100 }, (_, i) => ({ value: String(currentYear - i), label: String(currentYear - i) }));

            const daySelect = createSelect('0003_tag', dayOptions, getTranslation('0003_tag'));
            const monthSelect = createSelect('0003_monat', monthOptions, getTranslation('0003_monat'));
            const yearSelect = createSelect('0003_jahr', yearOptions, getTranslation('0003_jahr'));

            wrapper.appendChild(daySelect);
            wrapper.appendChild(monthSelect);
            wrapper.appendChild(yearSelect);

            return wrapper;
        }

        /**
         * Create standard input element
         */
        function createStandardInput(question) {
            let input;
            const currentAnswer = APP_STATE.answers[question.id];
            const container = document.createElement('div');

            switch (question.type) {
                case 'text':
                case 'number':
                    input = document.createElement('input');
                    input.type = question.type;
                    input. value = currentAnswer || '';
                    input.id = question.id;
                    input.name = question.id;
                    input.required = question.required;
                    
                    // Add real-time validation
                    input. addEventListener('blur', () => {
                        const errors = validateField(question, input. value);
                        showFieldError(question.id, errors);
                    });
                    
                    input.addEventListener('input', () => {
                        handleAnswerChange(input.id, input.value);
                        // Clear error on input
                        input.classList.remove('error');
                        const errorElement = document.getElementById(`${question.id}-error`);
                        if (errorElement) {
                            errorElement.classList. remove('visible');
                        }
                    });
                    
                    container.appendChild(input);
                    break;
                    
                case 'textarea':
                    input = document. createElement('textarea');
                    input.value = currentAnswer || '';
                    input.id = question. id;
                    input.name = question.id;
                    input.required = question.required;
                    
                    input.addEventListener('input', () => {
                        handleAnswerChange(input.id, input.value);
                    });
                    
                    container.appendChild(input);
                    break;
                    
                case 'select':
                    input = document.createElement('select');
                    input.id = question. id;
                    input.name = question.id;
                    input.required = question.required;
                    
                    const defaultOption = document.createElement('option');
                    defaultOption.value = '';
                    defaultOption.textContent = getTranslation('select_placeholder');
                    input.appendChild(defaultOption);

                    question.options.forEach(opt => {
                        const option = document. createElement('option');
                        option.value = opt.value;
                        option.textContent = getTranslation(opt.label_key || opt.value);
                        if (currentAnswer === opt.value) {
                            option.selected = true;
                        }
                        input.appendChild(option);
                    });
                    
                    input.addEventListener('change', () => {
                        handleAnswerChange(input. id, input.value);
                        const errors = validateField(question, input. value);
                        showFieldError(question.id, errors);
                    });
                    
                    container.appendChild(input);
                    break;
                    
                case 'multiselect':
                    input = document.createElement('div');
                    input.className = 'options-list';
                    
                    const selectedValues = Array.isArray(currentAnswer) ? currentAnswer : [];

                    question.options.forEach(opt => {
                        const item = document.createElement('div');
                        item.className = 'option-item';
                        if (selectedValues.includes(opt. value)) {
                            item. classList.add('selected');
                        }
                        
                        const checkbox = document.createElement('input');
                        checkbox.type = 'checkbox';
                        checkbox.id = `${question.id}-${opt.value}`;
                        checkbox.value = opt.value;
                        checkbox.checked = selectedValues.includes(opt. value);
                        
                        const label = document.createElement('span');
                        label.textContent = getTranslation(opt. label_key || opt.value);
                        
                        item.appendChild(checkbox);
                        item.appendChild(label);
                        
                        item.addEventListener('click', () => {
                            checkbox.checked = !checkbox.checked;
                            item.classList.toggle('selected', checkbox.checked);
                            
                            let newValues = Array.from(input.querySelectorAll('input: checked')).map(cb => cb.value);
                            handleAnswerChange(question.id, newValues);
                            renderCurrentSection();
                        });
                        
                        input.appendChild(item);
                    });
                    
                    container.appendChild(input);
                    return container;
                    
                default:
                    input = document. createElement('input');
                    input.type = 'text';
                    input. value = currentAnswer || '';
                    input.id = question.id;
                    input.name = question.id;
                    input.required = question.required;
                    
                    input.addEventListener('input', () => {
                        handleAnswerChange(input.id, input.value);
                    });
                    
                    container. appendChild(input);
            }
            
            // Add error message element (except for multiselect)
            if (question.type !== 'multiselect') {
                const errorMsg = document.createElement('div');
                errorMsg.className = 'error-message';
                errorMsg. id = `${question.id}-error`;
                container.appendChild(errorMsg);
            }
            
            return container;
        }

        /**
         * Render current section
         */
        function renderCurrentSection() {
            const section = APP_DATA.sections[APP_STATE.currentSectionIndex];
            const formContainer = document.getElementById('form-container');
            formContainer.innerHTML = '';

            const title = document.createElement('h2');
            title.textContent = getTranslation(section.id);
            formContainer.appendChild(title);

            section.questions.forEach(question => {
                const questionElement = document.createElement('div');
                questionElement.className = 'form-group';
                questionElement.id = `question-${question.id}`;
                
                const isVisible = checkCondition(question);
                
                if (! isVisible) {
                    questionElement.style.display = 'none';
                    delete APP_STATE.answers[question.id];
                    return;
                }

                questionElement.style.display = 'block';

                const label = document.createElement('label');
                label.className = 'question-label';
                label.innerHTML = getTranslation(question. id) + (question.required ? ' <span class="required-star">*</span>' : '');
                questionElement.appendChild(label);

                let inputElement;
                
                if (question.id. startsWith('0003_')) {
                    inputElement = createDateSelect(question);
                } else {
                    inputElement = createStandardInput(question);
                }

                questionElement.appendChild(inputElement);
                formContainer.appendChild(questionElement);
            });
            
            updateNavigationButtons();
        }

        /**
         * Update navigation buttons
         */
        function updateNavigationButtons() {
            const prevBtn = document.getElementById('prev-btn');
            const nextBtn = document.getElementById('next-btn');
            
            prevBtn.disabled = APP_STATE. currentSectionIndex === 0;
            nextBtn.textContent = getTranslation('btn_next');
        }

        /**
         * Update progress bar
         */
        function updateProgress() {
            const totalSections = APP_DATA.sections. length;
            const currentSection = APP_STATE.currentSectionIndex + 1;
            const progress = (currentSection / totalSections) * 100;
            
            document.getElementById('progress-fill').style.width = `${progress}%`;
            document.getElementById('progress-text').textContent = `Section ${currentSection} of ${totalSections}`;
        }

        /**
         * Handle answer change
         */
        function handleAnswerChange(id, value) {
            const sanitizedValue = Array.isArray(value) 
                ? value.map(sanitizeInput)
                : sanitizeInput(value);
            
            if (sanitizedValue === '' || (Array.isArray(sanitizedValue) && sanitizedValue.length === 0)) {
                delete APP_STATE.answers[id];
            } else {
                APP_STATE.answers[id] = sanitizedValue;
            }
            
            scheduleAutoSave();
        }

        // =================================================================
        // AUTO-SAVE FUNCTIONALITY
        // =================================================================
        
        let autoSaveTimer = null;

        function scheduleAutoSave() {
            if (autoSaveTimer) {
                clearTimeout(autoSaveTimer);
            }
            
            showSaveIndicator('saving');
            
            autoSaveTimer = setTimeout(async () => {
                try {
                    await saveToLocalStorage();
                    showSaveIndicator('saved');
                } catch (e) {
                    showSaveIndicator('error');
                    console.error('Auto-save failed:', e);
                }
            }, 2000);
        }

        function saveToLocalStorage() {
            return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
                try {
                    const saveData = {
                        answers:  APP_STATE.answers,
                        currentSection: APP_STATE.currentSectionIndex,
                        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
                    };
                    localStorage.setItem('anamnese_autosave', JSON.stringify(saveData));
                    resolve();
                } catch (e) {
                    reject(new Error('LocalStorage full or unavailable'));
                }
            });
        }

        function showSaveIndicator(status) {
            let indicator = document.getElementById('save-indicator');
            
            if (! indicator) {
                indicator = document.createElement('div');
                indicator.id = 'save-indicator';
                document.body.appendChild(indicator);
            }
            
            switch (status) {
                case 'saving':
                    indicator. textContent = '💾 Saving...';
                    indicator.style.backgroundColor = '#3b82f6';
                    indicator.style.color = 'white';
                    indicator.style.opacity = '1';
                    break;
                case 'saved':
                    indicator.textContent = '✓ Saved ' + new Date().toLocaleTimeString('en-US', {hour:  '2-digit', minute: '2-digit'});
                    indicator.style.backgroundColor = '#10b981';
                    indicator. style.color = 'white';
                    indicator.style.opacity = '1';
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        indicator. style.opacity = '0';
                    }, 2000);
                    break;
                case 'error':
                    indicator.textContent = '⚠️ Save failed';
                    indicator.style.backgroundColor = '#ef4444';
                    indicator.style.color = 'white';
                    indicator.style.opacity = '1';
                    break;
            }
        }

        function restoreAutoSave() {
            try {
                const savedData = localStorage.getItem('anamnese_autosave');
                if (savedData) {
                    const { answers, currentSection, timestamp } = JSON.parse(savedData);
                    const savedDate = new Date(timestamp);
                    const hoursSinceSave = (new Date() - savedDate) / 1000 / 3600;
                    
                    if (hoursSinceSave < 24) {
                        const restore = confirm(
                            `An incomplete questionnaire was found from ${savedDate.toLocaleString()}.\n\n` +
                            'Would you like to continue? '
                        );
                        
                        if (restore) {
                            APP_STATE.answers = answers;
                            APP_STATE.currentSectionIndex = currentSection;
                            return true;
                        }
                    }
                }
            } catch (e) {
                console.error('Failed to restore auto-save:', e);
            }
            return false;
        }

        // =================================================================
        // APPLICATION CONTROLLER
        // =================================================================
        
        const App = {
            init: async function() {
                try {
                    // Setup encryption
                    await setupEncryptionKey();
                    
                    // Restore auto-save if available
                    restoreAutoSave();
                    
                    // Update UI language
                    this.updateUILanguage();
                    
                    // Render first section
                    renderCurrentSection();
                    updateProgress();
                    
                } catch (e) {
                    console.error('Initialization error:', e);
                    alert('Failed to initialize application:  ' + e.message);
                }
            },
            
            changeLanguage: function(lang) {
                APP_STATE. currentLanguage = lang;
                
                // Update active language button
                document.querySelectorAll('.language-switcher button').forEach(btn => {
                    btn.classList.toggle('active', btn.dataset.lang === lang);
                });
                
                this.updateUILanguage();
                renderCurrentSection();
                updateProgress();
            },
            
            updateUILanguage: function() {
                document.getElementById('app-title').textContent = getTranslation('app_title');
                document.getElementById('app-subtitle').textContent = getTranslation('app_subtitle');
                document.getElementById('next-btn').textContent = getTranslation('btn_next');
                document.getElementById('prev-btn').textContent = getTranslation('btn_previous');
            },
            
            nextSection: function() {
                // Validate current section
                if (! validateCurrentSection()) {
                    alert(getTranslation('validation_required'));
                    return;
                }
                
                if (APP_STATE.currentSectionIndex < APP_DATA.sections. length - 1) {
                    APP_STATE.currentSectionIndex++;
                    renderCurrentSection();
                    updateProgress();
                    window.scrollTo(0, 0);
                } else {
                    // Final section - export data
                    this.exportData();
                }
            },
            
            previousSection: function() {
                if (APP_STATE.currentSectionIndex > 0) {
                    APP_STATE.currentSectionIndex--;
                    renderCurrentSection();
                    updateProgress();
                    window.scrollTo(0, 0);
                }
            },
            
            exportData:  async function() {
                const answerJson = {
                    metadata: {
                        version: APP_DATA.version,
                        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
                        language: APP_STATE.currentLanguage,
                        app_title: getTranslation('app_title')
                    },
                    answers: APP_STATE.answers
                };
                
                const jsonString = JSON.stringify(answerJson, null, 2);
                
                try {
                    const encryptedData = await encryptData(jsonString);
                    
                    const blob = new Blob([encryptedData], { type: 'text/plain' });
                    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
                    const a = document.createElement('a');
                    a.href = url;
                    a.download = 'anamnese_encrypted.txt';
                    document.body.appendChild(a);
                    a.click();
                    document.body.removeChild(a);
                    URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
                    
                    alert('✅ Data exported successfully!');
                } catch (e) {
                    console.error('Export error:', e);
                    alert('Export failed: ' + e.message);
                }
            }
        };

        // =================================================================
        // INITIALIZATION
        // =================================================================
        
        window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
            App.init();
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>
```

## Zusammenfassung der Änderungen:

### 1. **Test-Verschlüsselungsschlüssel**
- Neuer Test-Key hinzugefügt: `"MyTestKey12345678901234567890"` (genau 32 Zeichen)
- Dialog beim ersten Start fragt, ob Test-Key verwendet werden soll
- Für Produktion kann ein eigenes Passwort gesetzt werden

### 2. **Standardsprache auf Englisch**
- `APP_STATE.currentLanguage` auf `'en'` gesetzt
- Englisch-Button wird beim Start als `.active` markiert

### 3. **Sprachauswahl funktioniert jetzt**
- `changeLanguage()` Funktion aktualisiert alle UI-Elemente
- Aktiver Button wird visuell hervorgehoben
- Alle Texte werden sofort übersetzt

### 4. **Validierung mit Fehlermeldungen**
- Neue `validateField()` Funktion prüft: 
  - Pflichtfelder
  - Minimale Länge (z.B. 3 Zeichen für Nachname)
  - Regex-Muster (nur Buchstaben erlaubt)
- Fehlermeldungen erscheinen direkt unter den Feldern
- Rote Umrandung für fehlerhafte Felder
- "Next"-Button kann nur geklickt werden, wenn alle Felder korrekt sind

### 5. **OCR-Integration**
Die Tesseract. js und PDF. js Bibliotheken sind bereits im HTML eingebunden: 
```html
<script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/tesseract.js@5/dist/tesseract.min. js"></script>
<script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/pdfjs-dist@3.11.174/build/pdf.min.js"></script>

## Fix 1: Test-Verschlüsselungsschlüssel hinzufügen

Ersetzen Sie ab Zeile 478 die `setupEncryptionKey` Funktion: 

```javascript
// TEST KEY - genau 32 Zeichen für AES-256
const TEST_ENCRYPTION_KEY = "MyTestKey12345678901234567890";

async function setupEncryptionKey(retryCount = 0) {
    const MAX_RETRIES = 3;
    
    if (retryCount >= MAX_RETRIES) {
        alert('Maximale Anzahl an Versuchen überschritten.  Bitte laden Sie die Seite neu.');
        throw new Error('Max password attempts exceeded');
    }
    
    let storedKeyHash = localStorage.getItem('encryption_key_hash');
    
    if (!storedKeyHash) {
        // Erste Installation:  Test-Key für Entwicklung nutzen
        const useTestKey = confirm(
            'TEST MODE\n\n' +
            'Möchten Sie den Test-Schlüssel verwenden?\n' +
            '(Für Produktion "Abbrechen" klicken)'
        );
        
        let adminKey;
        if (useTestKey) {
            adminKey = TEST_ENCRYPTION_KEY;
        } else {
            adminKey = prompt(
                'WICHTIG: Erstmalige Einrichtung\n\n' +
                'Bitte geben Sie ein sicheres Master-Passwort ein (min.  16 Zeichen).\n' +
                'ACHTUNG: Wenn Sie dieses Passwort vergessen, sind alle Daten unwiederbringlich verloren!'
            );
            
            if (!adminKey || adminKey.length < 16) {
                alert('Passwort muss mindestens 16 Zeichen lang sein! ');
                return setupEncryptionKey(retryCount + 1);
            }
        }
        
        const keyHash = await crypto.subtle.digest(
            'SHA-256',
            new TextEncoder().encode(adminKey)
        );
        const keyHashHex = Array.from(new Uint8Array(keyHash))
            .map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2, '0'))
            .join('');
        
        localStorage.setItem('encryption_key_hash', keyHashHex);
        sessionStorage.setItem('derived_key', adminKey);
        
        alert('✅ Master-Passwort erfolgreich gesetzt!');
        return true;
    } else {
        if (! sessionStorage.getItem('derived_key')) {
            const enteredKey = prompt('Bitte geben Sie Ihr Master-Passwort ein:');
            
            if (!enteredKey) {
                alert('❌ Passwort erforderlich! ');
                return setupEncryptionKey(retryCount + 1);
            }
            
            const enteredHash = await crypto.subtle.digest(
                'SHA-256',
                new TextEncoder().encode(enteredKey)
            );
            const enteredHashHex = Array.from(new Uint8Array(enteredHash))
                .map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2, '0'))
                .join('');
            
            if (enteredHashHex !== storedKeyHash) {
                alert('❌ Falsches Passwort!');
                return setupEncryptionKey(retryCount + 1);
            }
            
            sessionStorage.setItem('derived_key', enteredKey);
        }
        return true;
    }
}
```

/**
 * Kompletter Neustart - löscht alle gespeicherten Daten
 */
function restartApplication() {
    const confirmRestart = confirm(
        'ACHTUNG: Alle gespeicherten Daten werden gelöscht!\n\n' +
        'Möchten Sie wirklich neu starten?'
    );
    
    if (confirmRestart) {
        // Lösche alle gespeicherten Daten
        localStorage.removeItem('anamnese_autosave');

        location.reload();

## Fix 4: Validierung mit Fehleranzeige

Fügen Sie diese Funktionen nach Zeile 436 hinzu:

```javascript
/**
 * Validiert ein einzelnes Feld
 */
function validateField(question, value) {
    const errors = [];
    
    // Pflichtfeld-Prüfung
    if (question.required && (! value || value === '' || (Array.isArray(value) && value.length === 0))) {
        errors.push(getTranslation('validation_required'));
    }
    
    // Wenn leer und nicht erforderlich, keine weiteren Prüfungen
    if (! value || value === '') {
        return errors;
    }
    
    // Validierungsregeln
    if (question.validation) {
        const { minLength, pattern } = question.validation;
        
        // Minimale Länge
        if (minLength && value.length < minLength) {
            errors.push(`Mindestens ${minLength} Zeichen erforderlich`);
        }
        
        // Pattern (Regex)
        if (pattern) {
            const regex = new RegExp(pattern);
            if (!regex.test(value)) {
                errors.push('Ungültiges Format.  Nur Buchstaben erlaubt');
            }
        }
    }
    
    return errors;
}

/**
 * Zeigt Fehler für ein Feld an
 */
function showFieldError(fieldId, errors) {
    const input = document.getElementById(fieldId);
    let errorElement = document.getElementById(`${fieldId}-error`);
    
    if (!errorElement) {
        errorElement = document.createElement('div');
        errorElement.id = `${fieldId}-error`;
        errorElement.style.color = '#ef4444';
        errorElement. style.fontSize = '13px';
        errorElement.style.marginTop = '5px';
        errorElement.style.fontWeight = '500';
        if (input && input.parentElement) {
            input.parentElement.appendChild(errorElement);
        }
    }
    
    if (input && errors.length > 0) {
        input.style.borderColor = '#ef4444';
        errorElement.textContent = errors[0];
        errorElement.style.display = 'block';
        return false;
    } else if (input) {
        input.style.borderColor = '';
        if (errorElement) {
            errorElement.style. display = 'none';
        }
        return true;
    }
    return true;
}

/**
 * Validiert alle sichtbaren Felder in der aktuellen Sektion
 */
function validateCurrentSection() {
    const section = APP_DATA.sections[APP_STATE.currentSectionIndex];
    let allValid = true;
    
    if (!section || !section.questions) return true;
    
    section.questions.forEach(question => {
        // Überspringe ausgeblendete Fragen
        if (! checkCondition(question)) {
            return;
        }
        
        const value = APP_STATE.answers[question.id];
        const errors = validateField(question, value);
        
        if (! showFieldError(question.id, errors)) {
            allValid = false;
        }
    });
    
    return allValid;
}
```

Ändern Sie in der `createStandardInput` Funktion (ab Zeile 307) für Text und Number Inputs:

case 'number':

    input.type = question.type;
    input.value = currentAnswer || '';
    input.id = question.id;
    input.name = question.id;
    input.required = question.required;
    
    // Echtzeit-Validierung
    input.addEventListener('blur', () => {
        const errors = validateField(question, input. value);
        showFieldError(question.id, errors);
    });
    
    input.addEventListener('input', () => {
        // Fehler beim Tippen ausblenden
        input.style.borderColor = '';
        const errorElement = document.getElementById(`${question.id}-error`);
        if (errorElement) {
            errorElement.style.display = 'none';
        }
    });
    break;

## Fix 5: OCR-Funktionalität komplett inline

Fügen Sie nach Zeile 27 (entfernen Sie `<script src="ocr-gdpr-module.js"></script>`) diesen Code hinzu:

```javascript
// =================================================================
// OCR FUNCTIONALITY - GDPR COMPLIANT
// =================================================================

/**
 * Initialisiert OCR Upload-Funktionalität
 */
function initOCRUpload() {
    const uploadArea = document.getElementById('file-upload-area');
    const fileInput = document.getElementById('file-input');
    
    if (!uploadArea || !fileInput) return;
    
    // Click to upload
    uploadArea.addEventListener('click', () => {
        fileInput.click();
    });
    
    // Drag & Drop
    uploadArea.addEventListener('dragover', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        uploadArea.classList.add('dragover');
    });
    
    uploadArea.addEventListener('dragleave', () => {
        uploadArea.classList.remove('dragover');
    });
    
    uploadArea.addEventListener('drop', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        uploadArea.classList.remove('dragover');
        
        const files = e.dataTransfer.files;
        if (files.length > 0) {
            handleFileUpload(files[0]);
        }
    });
    
    // File Input Change
    fileInput.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
        if (e.target.files.length > 0) {
            handleFileUpload(e.target. files[0]);
        }
    });
}

/**
 * Verarbeitet hochgeladene Datei
 */
async function handleFileUpload(file) {
    const progressDiv = document.getElementById('ocr-progress');
    const statusDiv = document.getElementById('ocr-status');
    
    if (!progressDiv || !statusDiv) return;
    
    progressDiv.classList.add('active');
    statusDiv.textContent = 'Dokument wird verarbeitet...';
    
    try {
        let extractedText = '';
        
        if (file.type === 'application/pdf') {
            extractedText = await extractTextFromPDF(file);
        } else if (file.type. startsWith('image/')) {
            extractedText = await extractTextFromImage(file);
        } else {
            throw new Error('Nicht unterstütztes Dateiformat');
        }
        
        // Text in Felder übertragen
        await mapTextToFields(extractedText);
        
        statusDiv.textContent = '✅ Dokument erfolgreich verarbeitet! ';
        setTimeout(() => {
            progressDiv. classList.remove('active');
        }, 3000);
        
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('OCR Error:', error);
        statusDiv.textContent = '❌ Fehler beim Verarbeiten:  ' + error.message;
        setTimeout(() => {
            progressDiv.classList.remove('active');
        }, 5000);
    }
}

/**
 * Extrahiert Text aus PDF
 */
async function extractTextFromPDF(file) {
    const arrayBuffer = await file.arrayBuffer();
    const pdf = await pdfjsLib.getDocument({ data: arrayBuffer }).promise;
    
    let fullText = '';
    
    for (let i = 1; i <= pdf.numPages; i++) {
        const page = await pdf.getPage(i);
        const textContent = await page.getTextContent();
        const pageText = textContent.items.map(item => item.str).join(' ');
        fullText += pageText + '\n';
    }
    
    return fullText;
}

/**
 * Extrahiert Text aus Bild (OCR)
 */
async function extractTextFromImage(file) {
    const { data: { text } } = await Tesseract.recognize(file, 'deu+eng', {
        logger: info => {
            const progress = document.getElementById('ocr-progress-fill');
            if (progress && info.status === 'recognizing text') {
                progress.style. width = `${info.progress * 100}%`;
            }
        }
    });
    
    return text;
}

/**
 * Mapt extrahierten Text auf Formularfelder
 */
async function mapTextToFields(text) {
    const lowerText = text.toLowerCase();
    
    // Name extrahieren
    const nameMatch = text.match(/name[:\s]+([a-zA-ZäöüÄÖÜß\s-]+)/i);
    if (nameMatch) {
        const fullName = nameMatch[1]. trim().split(' ');
        if (fullName.length >= 2) {
            APP_STATE. answers['0002_first_name'] = fullName[0];
            APP_STATE.answers['0002_last_name'] = fullName. slice(1).join(' ');
        }
    }
    
    // Geburtsdatum extrahieren (DD. MM.YYYY oder DD/MM/YYYY)
    const dateMatch = text.match(/(? :geburt|birth)[:\s]*(\d{1,2})[\./](\d{1,2})[\./](\d{4})/i);
    if (dateMatch) {
        APP_STATE.answers['0003_tag'] = dateMatch[1];
        APP_STATE.answers['0003_monat'] = dateMatch[2];
        APP_STATE.answers['0003_jahr'] = dateMatch[3];
    }
    
    // Geschlecht extrahieren
    if (lowerText.includes('herr') || lowerText.includes('male') || lowerText.includes('männlich')) {
        APP_STATE.answers['0001_salutation'] = 'mr';
    } else if (lowerText.includes('frau') || lowerText.includes('female') || lowerText.includes('weiblich')) {
        APP_STATE.answers['0001_salutation'] = 'ms';
    }
    
    // UI aktualisieren
    renderCurrentSection();
}
```

**Nach Zeile 469 (vor `async function setupEncryptionKey`) einfügen:**

const TEST_ENCRYPTION_KEY = "MyTestKey12345678901234567890";

**Zeilen 478-542 ERSETZEN (setupEncryptionKey Funktion):**
```javascript
async function setupEncryptionKey(retryCount = 0) {
    const MAX_RETRIES = 3;
    
    if (retryCount >= MAX_RETRIES) {
        alert('Maximale Anzahl an Versuchen überschritten.  Bitte laden Sie die Seite neu.');
        throw new Error('Max password attempts exceeded');
    }
    
    let storedKeyHash = localStorage.getItem('encryption_key_hash');
    
    if (!storedKeyHash) {
        // Erste Installation:  Test-Key Option
        const useTestKey = confirm(
            'TEST MODE\n\n' +
            'Möchten Sie den Test-Schlüssel verwenden?\n' +
            '(Für Produktion "Abbrechen" klicken)'
        );
        
        let adminKey;
        if (useTestKey) {
            adminKey = TEST_ENCRYPTION_KEY;
        } else {
            adminKey = prompt(
                'WICHTIG: Erstmalige Einrichtung\n\n' +
                'Bitte geben Sie ein sicheres Master-Passwort ein (min. 16 Zeichen).\n' +
                'ACHTUNG: Wenn Sie dieses Passwort vergessen, sind alle Daten unwiederbringlich verloren!'
            );
            
            if (!adminKey || adminKey.length < 16) {
                alert('Passwort muss mindestens 16 Zeichen lang sein! ');
                return setupEncryptionKey(retryCount + 1);
            }
        }
        
        const keyHash = await crypto.subtle.digest(
            'SHA-256',
            new TextEncoder().encode(adminKey)
        );
        const keyHashHex = Array.from(new Uint8Array(keyHash))
            .map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2, '0'))
            .join('');
        
        localStorage.setItem('encryption_key_hash', keyHashHex);
        sessionStorage.setItem('derived_key', adminKey);
        
        alert('✅ Master-Passwort erfolgreich gesetzt! ');
        return true;
    } else {
        if (! sessionStorage.getItem('derived_key')) {
            const enteredKey = prompt('Bitte geben Sie Ihr Master-Passwort ein: ');
            
            if (!enteredKey) {
                alert('❌ Passwort erforderlich!');
                return setupEncryptionKey(retryCount + 1);
            }
            
            const enteredHash = await crypto.subtle.digest(
                'SHA-256',
                new TextEncoder().encode(enteredKey)
            );
            const enteredHashHex = Array.from(new Uint8Array(enteredHash))
                .map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2, '0'))
                .join('');
            
            if (enteredHashHex !== storedKeyHash) {
                alert('❌ Falsches Passwort! ');
                return setupEncryptionKey(retryCount + 1);
            }
            
            sessionStorage.setItem('derived_key', enteredKey);
        }
        return true;
    }
}
```

/**
 * Kompletter Neustart - löscht alle gespeicherten Daten
 */
function restartApplication() {
    const confirmRestart = confirm(
        'ACHTUNG:  Alle gespeicherten Daten werden gelöscht!\n\n' +
        'Möchten Sie wirklich neu starten?'
    );
    
    if (confirmRestart) {
        // Lösche alle gespeicherten Daten
        localStorage.removeItem('anamnese_autosave');
        localStorage.removeItem('encryption_key_hash');
        sessionStorage.removeItem('derived_key');
        
        // Seite neu laden
        location.reload();
    }
}

### **Fix 4: Validierung mit Fehleranzeige** 
**Nach Zeile 436 EINFÜGEN:**
```javascript

// =================================================================
// VALIDATION FUNCTIONS
// =================================================================

/**
 * Validiert ein einzelnes Feld
 */
function validateField(question, value) {
    const errors = [];
    
    // Pflichtfeld-Prüfung
    if (question.required && (! value || value === '' || (Array.isArray(value) && value.length === 0))) {
        errors.push(getTranslation('validation_required'));
    }
    
    // Wenn leer und nicht erforderlich, keine weiteren Prüfungen
    if (! value || value === '') {
        return errors;
    }
    
    // Validierungsregeln
    if (question. validation) {
        const { minLength, pattern } = question.validation;
        
        // Minimale Länge
        if (minLength && value.length < minLength) {
            errors.push(`Mindestens ${minLength} Zeichen erforderlich`);
        }
        
        // Pattern (Regex)
        if (pattern) {
            const regex = new RegExp(pattern);
            if (!regex.test(value)) {
                errors.push('Ungültiges Format.  Nur Buchstaben erlaubt');
            }
        }
    }
    
    return errors;
}

/**
 * Zeigt Fehler für ein Feld an
 */
function showFieldError(fieldId, errors) {
    const input = document.getElementById(fieldId);
    let errorElement = document.getElementById(`${fieldId}-error`);
    
    if (!errorElement) {
        errorElement = document.createElement('div');
        errorElement. id = `${fieldId}-error`;
        errorElement.style.color = '#ef4444';
        errorElement. style.fontSize = '13px';
        errorElement.style.marginTop = '5px';
        errorElement.style.fontWeight = '500';
        if (input && input.parentElement) {
            input.parentElement.appendChild(errorElement);
        }
    }
    
    if (input && errors.length > 0) {
        input.style.borderColor = '#ef4444';
        errorElement.textContent = errors[0];
        errorElement.style.display = 'block';
        return false;
    } else if (input) {
        input.style.borderColor = '';
        if (errorElement) {
            errorElement.style. display = 'none';
        }
        return true;
    }
    return true;
}

/**
 * Validiert alle sichtbaren Felder in der aktuellen Sektion
 */
function validateCurrentSection() {
    const section = APP_DATA.sections[APP_STATE.currentSectionIndex];
    let allValid = true;
    
    if (!section || !section.questions) return true;
    
    section.questions.forEach(question => {
        // Überspringe ausgeblendete Fragen
        if (! checkCondition(question)) {
            return;
        }
        
        const value = APP_STATE.answers[question.id];
        const errors = validateField(question, value);
        
        if (! showFieldError(question.id, errors)) {
            allValid = false;
        }
    });
    
    return allValid;
}

Möchten Sie, dass ich eine **vollständige bereinigte Version** der gesamten Datei erstelle, oder können Sie diese Patches selbst einfügen? 
Perfekt! Ich erkläre Ihnen, wie diese komplexe bedingte Logik funktioniert und wie sie in Ihrer Datei implementiert werden muss: 

## 📋 **LOGIK-ERKLÄRUNG**

### **Konzept:  Verschachtelte bedingte Sektionen**

Die Logik funktioniert so: 

```
Section 1: Personal Info (0001-0003) → Immer anzeigen
    ↓
Section 2: Hauptfrage 1000 → Immer anzeigen
    ↓
    ├─ Wenn 1000 = "ja" → Section 3 (1001-1006) anzeigen
    │   ↓
    │   ├─ Wenn 1005 enthält "fieber" → Section 4a (1105-1405) anzeigen
    │   ├─ Wenn 1005 enthält "gewichtsverlust" → Section 4b (1505-1545) anzeigen
    │   │   └─ Wenn 1505 = "vermindert" → Fragen 1515-1545 anzeigen
    │   └─ Wenn 1005 enthält "kraftlosigkeit" → Section 4c (1805-1835) anzeigen
    │   
    │   └─ Wenn 1006 enthält "angio" → Section 5a (1010-1117) anzeigen
    │       ├─ Wenn 1010 enthält "gehstrecke" → 1110 anzeigen
    │       ├─ Wenn 1010 enthält "venen" → 1111 anzeigen
    │       ├─ Wenn 1010 enthält "oedem" → 1112 anzeigen
    │       └─ Wenn 1010 enthält "schmerz" → 1113-1115 anzeigen
    │
    └─ Wenn 1000 = "nein" → Springe zu Section 2000 (noch nicht definiert)
```

## 🔧 **IMPLEMENTIERUNG in APP_DATA**

### **Struktur:**

```javascript
const APP_DATA = {
    version: "8.0",
    sections: [
        // Section 1: Personal Info (immer angezeigt)
        {
            id: "personal_info",
            questions: [
                { id: "0001_salutation", type: "select", required: true, ...  },
                { id: "0002_first_name", type:  "text", required: true, ...  },
                { id: "0002_last_name", type: "text", required: true, ... },
                { id: "0003_tag", type: "select", required: true },
                { id: "0003_monat", type: "select", required: true },
                { id: "0003_jahr", type: "select", required: true }
            ]
        },
        
        // Section 2: Hauptfrage Beschwerden (immer angezeigt)
        {
            id: "complaints_main",
            questions: [
                {
                    id: "1000",
                    type: "select",
                    required: true,
                    options: [
                        { value: "ja", label_key: "option_yes" },
                        { value:  "nein", label_key:  "option_no" }
                    ]
                }
            ]
        },
        
        // Section 3: Details (nur wenn 1000 = ja)
        {
            id: "complaints_details",
            condition: {
                field: "1000",
                value: "ja",
                operator: "=="
            },
            questions: [

## 🔑 **WICHTIGE PUNKTE:**

### 1. **Section-Level Bedingungen:**
```javascript
{
    id: "section_name",
    condition: {
        field: "1000",      // Feld-ID
        value: "ja",        // Wert zum Vergleichen
        operator: "=="      // Operator
    },
    questions: [...]
}
```

### 2. **Question-Level Bedingungen (innerhalb einer Section):**
```javascript
{
    id: "1515",
    type: "number",
    condition: {
        field: "1505",
        value: "vermindert",
        operator: "=="
    }
}
```

### 3. **Operator-Typen:**
- `==` - Gleich (für Select)
- `!=` - Ungleich
- `includes` - **Enthält (für Multiselect/Checkbox)**
- `>`, `<`, `>=`, `<=` - Vergleiche (für Zahlen)

### 4. **Checkbox + Freitext Typ:**
Sie brauchen einen neuen Input-Typ:  `checkbox_freitext`

Fügen Sie in `createStandardInput` hinzu (nach Zeile 376):

```javascript
case 'checkbox_freitext': 
    const wrapper = document.createElement('div');
    
    // Checkboxen
    const checkboxDiv = document.createElement('div');
    checkboxDiv.className = 'options-list';
    
    const selectedValues = Array.isArray(currentAnswer) ? currentAnswer.filter(v => v !== 'freitext') : [];
    
    question.options.forEach(opt => {
        const item = document.createElement('div');
        item.className = 'option-item';
        if (selectedValues.includes(opt.value)) {
            item.classList.add('selected');
        }
        
        const checkbox = document.createElement('input');
        checkbox.type = 'checkbox';
        checkbox. id = `${question.id}-${opt.value}`;
        checkbox.value = opt.value;
        checkbox.checked = selectedValues.includes(opt.value);
        
        const label = document.createElement('span');
        label.textContent = getTranslation(opt.label_key || opt.value);
        
        item.appendChild(checkbox);
        item.appendChild(label);
        
        item.addEventListener('click', () => {
            checkbox.checked = !checkbox.checked;
            item.classList.toggle('selected', checkbox.checked);
            
            let newValues = Array.from(checkboxDiv.querySelectorAll('input: checked')).map(cb => cb.value);
            const freitextValue = freitextInput.value;
            if (freitextValue) {
                newValues. push('freitext: ' + freitextValue);
            }
            handleAnswerChange(question.id, newValues);
            renderCurrentSection();
        });
        
        checkboxDiv.appendChild(item);
    });
    
    wrapper.appendChild(checkboxDiv);
    
    // Freitext-Feld
    const freitextLabel = document.createElement('label');
    freitextLabel.textContent = getTranslation(question.freitext_label);
    freitextLabel.style.marginTop = '10px';
    freitextLabel.style.display = 'block';
    
    const freitextInput = document. createElement('input');
    freitextInput.type = 'text';
    freitextInput. id = `${question.id}-freitext`;
    freitextInput.placeholder = getTranslation(question.freitext_label);
    
    // Restore freitext value
    const freitextValue = currentAnswer?. find(v => typeof v === 'string' && v.startsWith('freitext:'));
    if (freitextValue) {
        freitextInput.value = freitextValue. replace('freitext:', '');
    }
    
    freitextInput.addEventListener('input', () => {
        let newValues = Array.from(checkboxDiv.querySelectorAll('input:checked')).map(cb => cb.value);
        if (freitextInput.value) {
            newValues.push('freitext:' + freitextInput.value);
        }
        handleAnswerChange(question.id, newValues);
    });
    
    wrapper.appendChild(freitextLabel);
    wrapper.appendChild(freitextInput);
    
    return wrapper;
```

## ✅ **ZUSAMMENFASSUNG:**

Ihre `checkCondition` Funktion (bereits vorhanden) prüft: 
1. **Section-Bedingungen** - Ganze Sektionen werden angezeigt/versteckt
2. **Question-Bedingungen** - Einzelne Fragen innerhalb einer Sektion werden angezeigt/versteckt
3. **Operator "includes"** - Funktioniert für Arrays (Multiselect, Checkboxen)

# 📋 **VOLLSTÄNDIGE IMPLEMENTIERUNGS-ANLEITUNG**

## **Struktur-Übersicht**

Ihre Logik hat **4 Hauptpfade**:

```
START (0000-0003)
    ↓
PFAD-AUSWAHL
    ├─ Termin → 1000 (Beschwerden) → 2000 (Terminvereinbarung)
    ├─ Rezept/Verordnung → 3003, 3004 (direkt zu Kontakt)
    └─ Sonstiges → 3003, 3004 (direkt zu Kontakt)
    
Falls 1000 = "ja": 
    → Beschwerde-Details (1001-1006)
        → Spezifische Beschwerde-Module (Angio, Atem, Magen, etc.)
        
Falls 1000 = "nein" ODER nach Beschwerden: 
    → 2000 (Terminvereinbarung)
        → 3000-3005 (Adressdaten, falls Neupatient)
        → 4000-4140 (Körpermaße, Impfungen, Lifestyle)
        → 5000-5003 (Diabetes, falls vorhanden)
        → 6000-6011 (Mobilität, Implantate, Allergien)
        → 7000-7011 (Begleiterkrankungen)
        → 8000-8900 (Vorerkrankungen, Operationen, Medikamente)
        → 9000-9900 (Kontakt-Check & Zufriedenheit)
```

### **3. Pädiatrische Fragen (nur wenn Alter < 7)**

Sie brauchen eine **Altersberechnung** aus `0003_jahr`:

```javascript
// Hilfsfunktion: Alter berechnen
function calculateAge() {
    const birthYear = parseInt(APP_STATE.answers['0003_jahr']);
    if (!birthYear) return null;
    const currentYear = new Date().getFullYear();
    return currentYear - birthYear;
}

// In checkCondition erweitern:
function checkCondition(item) {
    if (!item.condition) return true;
    
    const { field, value, operator = '==' } = item.condition;
    
    // SPEZIELL: Alters-Bedingung
    if (field === "age") {
        const age = calculateAge();
        if (age === null) return false;
        
        switch (operator) {
            case '<': return age < value;
            case '>': return age > value;
            case '<=': return age <= value;
            case '>=': return age >= value;
            case '==': return age == value;
            default: return false;
        }
    }
    
    // ...  Rest wie gehabt
}

// Beispiel Sektion: 
{
    id: "paediatric",
    condition: {
        field: "age",
        value: 7,
        operator: "<"
    },
    questions: [
        { id: "1P00_ernaehrung1LJ", type: "checkbox_freitext", ...  },
        // ... 
    ]
}
```

### **5. KOMBINIERTE Bedingungen (Alter + Geschlecht)**

Sie brauchen eine **erweiterte checkCondition**:

```javascript
function checkCondition(item) {
    if (!item.condition) return true;
    
    // MULTI-CONDITION SUPPORT
    if (Array.isArray(item.condition)) {
        // ALLE Bedingungen müssen erfüllt sein (AND)
        return item.condition.every(cond => checkSingleCondition(cond));
    }
    
    return checkSingleCondition(item. condition);
}

function checkSingleCondition(condition) {
    const { field, value, operator = '==' } = condition;
    
    // Alters-Check
    if (field === "age") {
        const age = calculateAge();
        if (age === null) return false;
        
        switch (operator) {
            case '<': return age < value;
            case '>': return age > value;
            case '<=': return age <= value;
            case '>=': return age >= value;
            case '==': return age == value;
            default:  return false;
        }
    }
    
    // Standard-Feld-Check
    const answer = APP_STATE.answers[field];
    if (answer === undefined || answer === null || answer === '') {
        return false;
    }
    
    // Array (Multiselect)
    if (Array.isArray(answer)) {
        if (operator === 'includes') {
            return answer.includes(value);
        }
        return false;
    }
    
    // Standard-Operatoren
    switch (operator) {
        case '==': return answer == value;
        case '!=': return answer != value;
        case '>': return parseFloat(answer) > parseFloat(value);
        case '<': return parseFloat(answer) < parseFloat(value);
        case '>=': return parseFloat(answer) >= parseFloat(value);
        case '<=': return parseFloat(answer) <= parseFloat(value);
        default: return false;
    }
}

// Beispiel:  Frage nur für Frauen ab 50
{
    id:  "mammography",
    condition: [
        {
            field: "0002",
            value: "weiblich",
            operator:  "=="
        },
        {
            field: "age",
            value: 50,
            operator: ">="
        }
    ],
    questions: [...]
}
```

### **3. Multiple Text Inputs (für 8006 - mehrfache Thrombosen)**

```javascript
case 'multiple_text':
    const wrapper = document.createElement('div');
    const values = Array.isArray(currentAnswer) ? currentAnswer : [''];
    
    values.forEach((val, idx) => {
        const row = document.createElement('div');
        row.style.marginBottom = '10px';
        
        const inp = document.createElement('input');
        inp.type = 'text';
        inp.value = val;
        inp.placeholder = getTranslation(question.placeholder_key || question.id);
        
        inp.addEventListener('input', () => {
            const allInputs = Array.from(wrapper.querySelectorAll('input')).map(i => i.value).filter(v => v);
            handleAnswerChange(question.id, allInputs);
        });
        
        row. appendChild(inp);
        wrapper.appendChild(row);
    });
    
    // Add-Button
    const addBtn = document. createElement('button');
    addBtn.type = 'button';
    addBtn.textContent = '+ Weitere hinzufügen';
    addBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        const newInput = document.createElement('input');
        newInput.type = 'text';
        const newRow = document.createElement('div');
        newRow.style.marginBottom = '10px';
        newRow.appendChild(newInput);
        wrapper.insertBefore(newRow, addBtn);
    });
    wrapper.appendChild(addBtn);
    
    return wrapper;
```

### **4. Star Rating (für 9900)**

```javascript
case 'rating':
    const ratingWrapper = document.createElement('div');
    ratingWrapper.className = 'rating-stars';
    
    for (let i = 1; i <= 5; i++) {
        const star = document.createElement('span');
        star.textContent = '★';
        star.className = 'star';
        star. dataset.value = i;
        
        if (currentAnswer && i <= currentAnswer) {
            star.classList.add('selected');
        }
        
        star. addEventListener('click', () => {
            handleAnswerChange(question.id, i);
            ratingWrapper.querySelectorAll('.star').forEach((s, idx) => {
                s.classList.toggle('selected', idx < i);
            });
        });
        
        ratingWrapper. appendChild(star);
    }
    
    return ratingWrapper;
```

**CSS für Stars:**

```css
.rating-stars {

}

    cursor: pointer;

}

}

## **🎬 NAVIGATION-LOGIK**

Für das **Überspringen** von Sektionen:

```javascript
function getNextVisibleSection(currentIndex) {
    for (let i = currentIndex + 1; i < APP_DATA. sections.length; i++) {
        const section = APP_DATA.sections[i];
        
        // Prüfe Section-Bedingung
        if (checkCondition(section)) {
            return i;
        }
    }
    return -1; // Keine weitere Sektion
}

function getPreviousVisibleSection(currentIndex) {
    for (let i = currentIndex - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
        const section = APP_DATA.sections[i];
        
        if (checkCondition(section)) {
            return i;
        }
    }
    return 0; // Erste Sektion
}

// In nextSection():
function nextSection() {
    if (! validateCurrentSection()) {
        alert(getTranslation('validation_required'));
        return;
    }
    
    const nextIndex = getNextVisibleSection(APP_STATE.currentSectionIndex);
    
    if (nextIndex === -1) {
        // Fragebogen abgeschlossen
        showCompletionScreen();
    } else {
        APP_STATE.currentSectionIndex = nextIndex;
        renderCurrentSection();
        updateProgress();
        window.scrollTo(0, 0);
    }
}

// In previousSection():
function previousSection() {
    const prevIndex = getPreviousVisibleSection(APP_STATE.currentSectionIndex);
    APP_STATE.currentSectionIndex = prevIndex;
    renderCurrentSection();
    updateProgress();
    window.scrollTo(0, 0);
}
```

```javascript
function checkCondition(item) {
    if (!item. condition) return true;
    
    // Multi-condition support
    if (Array.isArray(item.condition)) {
        return item.condition. every(cond => checkSingleCondition(cond));
    }
    
    return checkSingleCondition(item. condition);
}

function checkSingleCondition(condition) {
    const { field, value, operator = '==' } = condition;
    
    // Age calculation
    if (field === "age") {
        const age = calculateAge();
        if (age === null) return false;
        // ... age checks
    }
    
    // Standard field checks
    // ... existing logic
}

function calculateAge() {
    const birthYear = parseInt(APP_STATE.answers['0003_jahr']);
    if (! birthYear) return null;
    return new Date().getFullYear() - birthYear;
}
```

### **3.2 JavaScript-Bereich (Zeilen 28-1543)**

#### **➕ Nach Zeile 25 (VOR altem Script-Tag) - OCR inline:**
```javascript
<script>
// =================================================================
// OCR FUNCTIONALITY - GDPR COMPLIANT (INLINE)
// =================================================================

function initOCRUpload() {
    const uploadArea = document.getElementById('file-upload-area');
    const fileInput = document.getElementById('file-input');
    
    if (! uploadArea || !fileInput) return;
    
    uploadArea. addEventListener('click', () => fileInput.click());
    
    uploadArea.addEventListener('dragover', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        uploadArea.classList.add('dragover');
    });
    
    uploadArea.addEventListener('dragleave', () => {
        uploadArea.classList.remove('dragover');
    });
    
    uploadArea.addEventListener('drop', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        uploadArea.classList.remove('dragover');
        if (e.dataTransfer.files.length > 0) {
            handleFileUpload(e.dataTransfer.files[0]);
        }
    });
    
    fileInput.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
        if (e.target.files.length > 0) {
            handleFileUpload(e.target. files[0]);
        }
    });
}

async function handleFileUpload(file) {
    const progressDiv = document.getElementById('ocr-progress');
    const statusDiv = document.getElementById('ocr-status');
    const progressFill = document.getElementById('ocr-progress-fill');
    
    if (!progressDiv || !statusDiv) return;
    
    progressDiv.classList.add('active');
    statusDiv.textContent = 'Processing document...';
    
    try {
        let extractedText = '';
        
        if (file.type === 'application/pdf') {
            extractedText = await extractTextFromPDF(file);
        } else if (file.type. startsWith('image/')) {
            extractedText = await extractTextFromImage(file, progressFill);
        } else {
            throw new Error('Unsupported file format');
        }
        
        await mapTextToFields(extractedText);
        
        statusDiv.textContent = '✅ Document processed successfully! ';
        setTimeout(() => {
            progressDiv. classList.remove('active');
        }, 3000);
        
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('OCR Error:', error);
        statusDiv. textContent = '❌ Processing error:  ' + error.message;
        setTimeout(() => {
            progressDiv. classList.remove('active');
        }, 5000);
    }
}

async function extractTextFromPDF(file) {
    const arrayBuffer = await file.arrayBuffer();
    const pdf = await pdfjsLib.getDocument({ data: arrayBuffer }).promise;
    
    let fullText = '';
    for (let i = 1; i <= pdf.numPages; i++) {
        const page = await pdf.getPage(i);
        const textContent = await page.getTextContent();
        const pageText = textContent.items.map(item => item.str).join(' ');
        fullText += pageText + '\n';
    }
    
    return fullText;
}

async function extractTextFromImage(file, progressElement) {
    const { data:  { text } } = await Tesseract.recognize(file, 'deu+eng', {
        logger: info => {
            if (progressElement && info.status === 'recognizing text') {
                progressElement.style.width = `${info.progress * 100}%`;
            }
        }
    });
    
    return text;
}

async function mapTextToFields(text) {
    const lowerText = text.toLowerCase();
    
    // Name extrahieren
    const nameMatch = text.match(/name[:\s]+([a-zA-ZäöüÄÖÜß\s-]+)/i);
    if (nameMatch) {
        const fullName = nameMatch[1]. trim().split(' ');
        if (fullName.length >= 2) {
            APP_STATE. answers['0002_first_name'] = fullName[0];
            APP_STATE.answers['0002_last_name'] = fullName. slice(1).join(' ');
        }
    }
    
    // Geburtsdatum (DD.MM.YYYY oder DD/MM/YYYY)
    const dateMatch = text.match(/(? :geburt|birth)[:\s]*(\d{1,2})[\./](\d{1,2})[\./](\d{4})/i);
    if (dateMatch) {
        APP_STATE.answers['0003_tag'] = dateMatch[1];
        APP_STATE.answers['0003_monat'] = dateMatch[2];
        APP_STATE.answers['0003_jahr'] = dateMatch[3];
    }
    
    // Geschlecht
    if (lowerText.includes('herr') || lowerText.includes('male') || lowerText.includes('männlich')) {
        APP_STATE.answers['0002'] = 'maennlich';
    } else if (lowerText.includes('frau') || lowerText.includes('female') || lowerText.includes('weiblich')) {
        APP_STATE.answers['0002'] = 'weiblich';
    }
    
    renderCurrentSection();
}
</script>
```

#### **➕ Nach Zeile 27 (nach gelöschtem ocr-module) - APP_DATA + APP_STATE:**
```javascript
<script>

                    ]
