#### **❌ Zeilen 38-78 - Erste checkCondition LÖSCHEN** (Duplikat)

#### **✏️ Zeilen 102-142 - checkCondition ERSETZEN mit Multi-Support:**
```javascript
/**
 * Überprüft Bedingungen (Single oder Multi)
 */
function checkCondition(item) {
    if (! item.condition) return true;
    
    // Multi-Condition Support (Array von Bedingungen)
    if (Array.isArray(item. condition)) {
        return item. condition.every(cond => checkSingleCondition(cond));
    }
    
    return checkSingleCondition(item. condition);
}

function checkSingleCondition(condition) {
    const { field, value, operator = '==' } = condition;
    
    // Spezialfall: Altersberechnung
    if (field === "age") {
        const age = calculateAge();
        if (age === null) return false;
        
        switch (operator) {
            case '<':  return age < value;
            case '>': return age > value;
            case '<=': return age <= value;
            case '>=': return age >= value;
            case '==': return age == value;
            default: return false;
        }
    }
    
    // Standard-Feld-Check
    const answer = APP_STATE.answers[field];
    if (answer === undefined || answer === null || answer === '') {
        return false;
    }
    
    // Array-Check (Multiselect)
    if (Array.isArray(answer)) {
        if (operator === 'includes') {
            return answer.includes(value);
        }
        return false;
    }
    
    // Standard-Operatoren
    switch (operator) {
        case '==': return answer == value;
        case '!=': return answer != value;
        case '>': return parseFloat(answer) > parseFloat(value);
        case '<': return parseFloat(answer) < parseFloat(value);
        case '>=': return parseFloat(answer) >= parseFloat(value);
        case '<=': return parseFloat(answer) <= parseFloat(value);
        default: return false;
    }
}

function calculateAge() {
    const birthYear = parseInt(APP_STATE.answers['0003_jahr']);
    if (! birthYear) return null;
    return new Date().getFullYear() - birthYear;
}
```

#### **➕ Nach Zeile 436 - Validierung einfügen:**
```javascript
// =================================================================
// VALIDATION FUNCTIONS
// =================================================================

function validateField(question, value) {
    const errors = [];
    
    if (question.required && (! value || value === '' || (Array.isArray(value) && value.length === 0))) {
        errors.push(getTranslation('validation_required'));
    }
    
    if (! value || value === '') return errors;
    
    if (question.validation) {
        const { minLength, pattern, type } = question.validation;
        
        if (minLength && value.length < minLength) {
            errors.push(getTranslation('validation_min_length').replace('{min}', minLength));
        }
        
        if (pattern) {
            const regex = new RegExp(pattern);
            if (!regex.test(value)) {
                errors.push(getTranslation('validation_pattern'));
            }
        }
        
        if (type === 'email') {
            const emailRegex = /^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/;
            if (!emailRegex.test(value)) {
                errors.push(getTranslation('validation_email'));
            }
        }
        
        if (type === 'phone') {
            const phoneRegex = /^\+?[0-9\s\-()]+$/;
            if (!phoneRegex.test(value)) {
                errors.push(getTranslation('validation_phone'));
            }
        }
    }
    
    return errors;
}

function showFieldError(fieldId, errors) {
    const input = document.getElementById(fieldId);
    let errorElement = document.getElementById(`${fieldId}-error`);
    
    if (!errorElement) {
        errorElement = document. createElement('div');
        errorElement.id = `${fieldId}-error`;
        errorElement.className = 'error-message';
        if (input && input.parentElement) {
            input.parentElement.appendChild(errorElement);
        }
    }
    
    if (input && errors.length > 0) {
        input.classList.add('error');
        errorElement.textContent = errors[0];
        errorElement.classList.add('visible');
        return false;
    } else if (input) {
        input.classList.remove('error');
        if (errorElement) {
            errorElement.classList. remove('visible');
        }
        return true;
    }
    return true;
}

function validateCurrentSection() {
    const section = APP_DATA.sections[APP_STATE.currentSectionIndex];
    let allValid = true;
    
    if (!section || !section.questions) return true;
    
    section.questions.forEach(question => {
        if (!checkCondition(question)) return;
        
        const value = APP_STATE.answers[question.id];
        const errors = validateField(question, value);
        
        if (! showFieldError(question.id, errors)) {
            allValid = false;
        }
    });
    
    return allValid;
}
```

```javascript
/**
 * Kompletter Neustart - löscht alle Daten
 */
function restartApplication() {
    const confirmRestart = confirm(
        'WARNING: All saved data will be deleted!\n\n' +
        'Do you really want to restart? '
    );
    
    if (confirmRestart) {
        localStorage.removeItem('anamnese_autosave');
        localStorage.removeItem('encryption_key_hash');
        sessionStorage.removeItem('derived_key');
        location.reload();
    }
}
```

#### **➕ Nach App. previousSection (~1530) - Navigation:**
```javascript
function getNextVisibleSection(currentIndex) {
    for (let i = currentIndex + 1; i < APP_DATA. sections.length; i++) {
        if (checkCondition(APP_DATA.sections[i])) {
            return i;
        }
    }
    return -1;
}

function getPreviousVisibleSection(currentIndex) {
    for (let i = currentIndex - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
        if (checkCondition(APP_DATA.sections[i])) {
            return i;
        }
    }
    return 0;
}
```

- **Option A**: "Weiter mit Teil 2" (übersichtlicher, 4 Teile)
- **Option B**: "Alles in einer Datei" (eine große Datei, schwerer zu reviewen)

Perfekt! Dann machen wir das systematisch in 10 Teilen. Hier kommt:

# 🚀 **TEIL 3/10: APP_DATA - Beschwerde-Sektionen (Angio, Atem, Magen, etc.)**

```html
// =================================================================
// OCR FUNKTIONALITÄT - INLINE (GDPR-COMPLIANT)
// =================================================================

/**
 * Initialisiert OCR Upload-Funktionalität
 */
function initOCRUpload() {
    const uploadArea = document.getElementById('file-upload-area');
    const fileInput = document.getElementById('file-input');
    
    if (!uploadArea || !fileInput) return;
    
    // Click to upload
    uploadArea.addEventListener('click', () => {
        fileInput.click();
    });
    
    // Drag & Drop
    uploadArea.addEventListener('dragover', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        uploadArea.classList.add('dragover');
    });
    
    uploadArea.addEventListener('dragleave', () => {
        uploadArea.classList.remove('dragover');
    });
    
    uploadArea.addEventListener('drop', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        uploadArea.classList.remove('dragover');
        
        const files = e.dataTransfer.files;
        if (files.length > 0) {
            handleFileUpload(files[0]);
        }
    });
    
    // File Input Change
    fileInput.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
        if (e.target.files.length > 0) {
            handleFileUpload(e.target. files[0]);
        }
    });
}

/**
 * Verarbeitet hochgeladene Datei
 */
async function handleFileUpload(file) {
    const progressDiv = document.getElementById('ocr-progress');
    const statusDiv = document.getElementById('ocr-status');
    const progressFill = document.getElementById('ocr-progress-fill');
    
    if (!progressDiv || !statusDiv) return;
    
    progressDiv.classList.add('active');
    statusDiv.textContent = getTranslation('ocr_processing') || 'Processing document...';
    
    try {
        let extractedText = '';
        
        if (file.type === 'application/pdf') {
            extractedText = await extractTextFromPDF(file);
        } else if (file.type. startsWith('image/')) {
            extractedText = await extractTextFromImage(file, progressFill);
        } else {
            throw new Error(getTranslation('ocr_unsupported_format') || 'Unsupported file format');
        }
        
        // Text in Felder übertragen
        await mapTextToFields(extractedText);
        
        statusDiv.textContent = getTranslation('ocr_success') || '✅ Document processed successfully! ';
        setTimeout(() => {
            progressDiv. classList.remove('active');
        }, 3000);
        
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('OCR Error:', error);
        statusDiv.textContent = (getTranslation('ocr_error') || '❌ Processing error:  ') + error.message;
        setTimeout(() => {
            progressDiv.classList.remove('active');
        }, 5000);
    }
}

/**
 * Extrahiert Text aus PDF
 */
async function extractTextFromPDF(file) {
    const arrayBuffer = await file.arrayBuffer();
    const pdf = await pdfjsLib.getDocument({ data: arrayBuffer }).promise;
    
    let fullText = '';
    
    for (let i = 1; i <= pdf.numPages; i++) {
        const page = await pdf.getPage(i);
        const textContent = await page.getTextContent();
        const pageText = textContent.items. map(item => item.str).join(' ');
        fullText += pageText + '\n';
    }
    
    return fullText;
}

/**
 * Extrahiert Text aus Bild (OCR)
 */
async function extractTextFromImage(file, progressElement) {
    const { data:  { text } } = await Tesseract.recognize(file, 'deu+eng+fra', {
        logger: info => {
            if (progressElement && info.status === 'recognizing text') {
                progressElement.style.width = `${info.progress * 100}%`;
            }
        }
    });
    
    return text;
}

/**
 * Mapt extrahierten Text auf Formularfelder
 */
async function mapTextToFields(text) {
    const lowerText = text.toLowerCase();
    
    // Name extrahieren (verschiedene Muster)
    const namePatterns = [
        /name[:\s]+([a-zA-ZäöüÄÖÜß\s-]+)/i,
        /nachname[:\s]+([a-zA-ZäöüÄÖÜß\s-]+)/i,
        /surname[:\s]+([a-zA-Z\s-]+)/i
    ];
    
    for (const pattern of namePatterns) {
        const nameMatch = text.match(pattern);
        if (nameMatch) {
            const fullName = nameMatch[1].trim().split(/\s+/);
            if (fullName.length >= 2) {
                APP_STATE.answers['0001'] = fullName[0];  // Vorname
                APP_STATE. answers['0000'] = fullName. slice(1).join(' ');  // Nachname
                break;
            }
        }
    }
    
    // Geburtsdatum extrahieren (DD. MM.YYYY oder DD/MM/YYYY oder DD-MM-YYYY)
    const datePatterns = [
        /(? :geburt|birth|date.*birth)[:\s]*(\d{1,2})[\./\-](\d{1,2})[\./\-](\d{4})/i,
        /(\d{1,2})[\./\-](\d{1,2})[\./\-](\d{4})/
    ];
    
    for (const pattern of datePatterns) {
        const dateMatch = text. match(pattern);
        if (dateMatch) {
            APP_STATE.answers['0003_tag'] = dateMatch[1];
            APP_STATE.answers['0003_monat'] = dateMatch[2];
            APP_STATE.answers['0003_jahr'] = dateMatch[3];
            break;
        }
    }
    
    // Geschlecht extrahieren
    if (lowerText.includes('herr') || lowerText.includes('male') || lowerText.includes('männlich') || lowerText.includes('m/')) {
        APP_STATE.answers['0002'] = 'maennlich';
    } else if (lowerText.includes('frau') || lowerText.includes('female') || lowerText.includes('weiblich') || lowerText.includes('f/')) {
        APP_STATE.answers['0002'] = 'weiblich';
    }
    
    // PLZ und Ort extrahieren
    const addressMatch = text.match(/(\d{5})\s+([a-zA-ZäöüÄÖÜß\s-]+)/);
    if (addressMatch) {
        APP_STATE.answers['3000'] = addressMatch[1];  // PLZ
        APP_STATE.answers['3001'] = addressMatch[2]. trim();  // Ort
    }
    
    // E-Mail extrahieren
    const emailMatch = text.match(/([a-zA-Z0-9._-]+@[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+\.[a-zA-Z0-9_-]+)/);
    if (emailMatch) {
        APP_STATE.answers['3003'] = emailMatch[1];
        APP_STATE.answers['9000'] = emailMatch[1];  // Auch für Bestätigung
    }
    
    // Telefonnummer extrahieren
    const phoneMatch = text.match(/(\+?\d{1,4}[\s\-]?\(?\d{1,5}\)?[\s\-]?\d{1,10}[\s\-]?\d{0,10})/);
    if (phoneMatch) {
        APP_STATE.answers['3004'] = phoneMatch[1];
        APP_STATE.answers['9001'] = phoneMatch[1];  // Auch für Bestätigung
    }
    
    // UI aktualisieren
    renderCurrentSection();
    updateProgress();
}

// =================================================================
// TEST ENCRYPTION KEY + VERSCHLÜSSELUNG
// =================================================================

// TEST ENCRYPTION KEY (32 Zeichen für AES-256)
const TEST_ENCRYPTION_KEY = "MyTestKey12345678901234567890";

/**
 * Setup encryption key - mit Test-Key Option
 */
async function setupEncryptionKey(retryCount = 0) {
    const MAX_RETRIES = 3;
    
    if (retryCount >= MAX_RETRIES) {
        alert(getTranslation('encryption_max_retries') || 'Maximale Anzahl an Versuchen überschritten.  Bitte laden Sie die Seite neu.');
        throw new Error('Max password attempts exceeded');
    }
    
    let storedKeyHash = localStorage.getItem('encryption_key_hash');
    
    if (!storedKeyHash) {
        // Erste Installation:  Test-Key Option
        const useTestKey = confirm(
            getTranslation('encryption_test_mode') || 
            'TEST MODE\n\nMöchten Sie den Test-Schlüssel verwenden?\n(Für Produktion "Abbrechen" klicken)'
        );
        
        let adminKey;
        if (useTestKey) {
            adminKey = TEST_ENCRYPTION_KEY;
        } else {
            adminKey = prompt(
                getTranslation('encryption_first_setup') ||
                'WICHTIG: Erstmalige Einrichtung\n\n' +
                'Bitte geben Sie ein sicheres Master-Passwort ein (min. 16 Zeichen).\n' +
                'ACHTUNG: Wenn Sie dieses Passwort vergessen, sind alle Daten unwiederbringlich verloren!'
            );
            
            if (!adminKey || adminKey.length < 16) {
                alert(getTranslation('encryption_min_length') || 'Passwort muss mindestens 16 Zeichen lang sein! ');
                return setupEncryptionKey(retryCount + 1);
            }
        }
        
        // Hash für Verifikation speichern (NICHT das Passwort!)
        const keyHash = await crypto.subtle.digest(
            'SHA-256',
            new TextEncoder().encode(adminKey)
        );
        const keyHashHex = Array.from(new Uint8Array(keyHash))
            .map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2, '0'))
            .join('');
        
        localStorage.setItem('encryption_key_hash', keyHashHex);
        sessionStorage.setItem('derived_key', adminKey);
        
        alert(getTranslation('encryption_success') || '✅ Master-Passwort erfolgreich gesetzt!');
        return true;
    } else {
        // Key existiert:  Bei Start erneut abfragen
        if (! sessionStorage.getItem('derived_key')) {
            const enteredKey = prompt(getTranslation('encryption_enter_password') || 'Bitte geben Sie Ihr Master-Passwort ein:');
            
            if (!enteredKey) {
                alert(getTranslation('encryption_required') || '❌ Passwort erforderlich!');
                return setupEncryptionKey(retryCount + 1);
            }
            
            const enteredHash = await crypto.subtle.digest(
                'SHA-256',
                new TextEncoder().encode(enteredKey)
            );
            const enteredHashHex = Array.from(new Uint8Array(enteredHash))
                .map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2, '0'))
                .join('');
            
            if (enteredHashHex !== storedKeyHash) {
                alert(getTranslation('encryption_wrong_password') || '❌ Falsches Passwort! ');
                return setupEncryptionKey(retryCount + 1);
            }
            
            sessionStorage.setItem('derived_key', enteredKey);
        }
        return true;
    }
}

</script>
```

# 🚀 **TEIL 9/10: Multi-Condition, Validierung, Neue Input-Typen, Navigation**

```html
<script>
// =================================================================
// MULTI-CONDITION SUPPORT & ALTERSBERECHNUNG
// =================================================================

/**
 * Berechnet das Alter aus dem Geburtsjahr
 * @returns {number|null} - Das Alter oder null
 */
function calculateAge() {
    const birthYear = parseInt(APP_STATE.answers['0003_jahr']);
    if (! birthYear || isNaN(birthYear)) return null;
    
    const currentYear = new Date().getFullYear();
    const age = currentYear - birthYear;
    
    // Optional: Genauere Berechnung mit Tag/Monat
    const birthMonth = parseInt(APP_STATE. answers['0003_monat']);
    const birthDay = parseInt(APP_STATE.answers['0003_tag']);
    
    if (birthMonth && birthDay) {
        const currentDate = new Date();
        const currentMonth = currentDate.getMonth() + 1;
        const currentDay = currentDate.getDate();
        
        if (currentMonth < birthMonth || (currentMonth === birthMonth && currentDay < birthDay)) {
            return age - 1;
        }
    }
    
    return age;
}

/**
 * Überprüft Bedingungen (Single oder Multi-Condition)
 * @param {object} item - Sektion oder Frage mit optionaler 'condition'
 * @returns {boolean} - True wenn Bedingung erfüllt
 */
function checkCondition(item) {
    if (!item.condition) return true;
    
    // Multi-Condition Support (Array von Bedingungen - alle müssen erfüllt sein)
    if (Array.isArray(item.condition)) {
        return item.condition.every(cond => checkSingleCondition(cond));
    }
    
    return checkSingleCondition(item. condition);
}

/**
 * Überprüft eine einzelne Bedingung
 * @param {object} condition - Die Bedingung
 * @returns {boolean} - True wenn erfüllt
 */
function checkSingleCondition(condition) {
    const { field, value, operator = '==' } = condition;
    
    // SPEZIALFALL: Altersberechnung
    if (field === "age") {
        const age = calculateAge();
        if (age === null) return false;
        
        switch (operator) {
            case '<':  return age < value;
            case '>': return age > value;
            case '<=': return age <= value;
            case '>=': return age >= value;
            case '==': return age == value;
            case '!=':  return age != value;
            default: return false;
        }
    }
    
    // Standard-Feld-Check
    const answer = APP_STATE.answers[field];
    
    // Wenn keine Antwort vorhanden, Bedingung nicht erfüllt
    if (answer === undefined || answer === null || answer === '') {
        return false;
    }
    
    // Array-Check (Multiselect/Checkbox)
    if (Array.isArray(answer)) {
        if (operator === 'includes') {
            // Prüfe ob der Wert im Array enthalten ist
            return answer.includes(value);
        }
        // Für andere Operatoren bei Arrays:  nicht unterstützt
        return false;
    }
    
    // Standard-Operatoren
    switch (operator) {
        case '==': 
            return answer == value;
        case '!=':
            return answer != value;
        case '>':
            return parseFloat(answer) > parseFloat(value);
        case '<':
            return parseFloat(answer) < parseFloat(value);
        case '>=':
            return parseFloat(answer) >= parseFloat(value);
        case '<=': 
            return parseFloat(answer) <= parseFloat(value);
        default:
            return false;
    }
}

// =================================================================
// VALIDIERUNGS-FUNKTIONEN
// =================================================================

/**
 * Validiert ein einzelnes Feld
 * @param {object} question - Das Fragenobjekt
 * @param {*} value - Der Wert zum Validieren
 * @returns {Array} - Array von Fehlermeldungen
 */
function validateField(question, value) {
    const errors = [];
    
    // Pflichtfeld-Prüfung
    if (question.required) {
        if (!value || value === '' || (Array.isArray(value) && value.length === 0)) {
            errors.push(getTranslation('validation_required'));
            return errors; // Keine weiteren Checks wenn leer und required
        }
    }
    
    // Wenn leer und nicht required, keine weiteren Prüfungen
    if (!value || value === '') {
        return errors;
    }
    
    // Validierungsregeln
    if (question.validation) {
        const { minLength, maxLength, pattern, type, min, max } = question.validation;
        
        // Minimale Länge
        if (minLength && value.length < minLength) {
            const msg = getTranslation('validation_min_length').replace('{min}', minLength);
            errors.push(msg);
        }
        
        // Maximale Länge
        if (maxLength && value.length > maxLength) {
            const msg = getTranslation('validation_max_length').replace('{max}', maxLength);
            errors.push(msg);
        }
        
        // Pattern (Regex)
        if (pattern) {
            const regex = new RegExp(pattern);
            if (!regex.test(value)) {
                errors.push(getTranslation('validation_pattern'));
            }
        }
        
        // Numerische Validierung
        if (type === 'number' || question.type === 'number') {
            const numValue = parseFloat(value);
            
            if (isNaN(numValue)) {
                errors.push(getTranslation('validation_number'));
            } else {
                if (min !== undefined && numValue < min) {
                    const msg = getTranslation('validation_min').replace('{min}', min);
                    errors. push(msg);
                }
                if (max !== undefined && numValue > max) {
                    const msg = getTranslation('validation_max').replace('{max}', max);
                    errors.push(msg);
                }
            }
        }
        
        // E-Mail Validierung
        if (type === 'email' || question.type === 'email') {
            const emailRegex = /^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/;
            if (!emailRegex.test(value)) {
                errors.push(getTranslation('validation_email'));
            }
        }
        
        // Telefon Validierung
        if (type === 'phone' || question.type === 'tel') {
            const phoneRegex = /^\+?[0-9\s\-()]+$/;
            if (!phoneRegex.test(value)) {
                errors.push(getTranslation('validation_phone'));
            }
        }
    }
    
    return errors;
}

/**
 * Zeigt Fehler für ein Feld an
 * @param {string} fieldId - Die Feld-ID
 * @param {Array} errors - Array von Fehlermeldungen
 * @returns {boolean} - True wenn valide (keine Fehler)
 */
function showFieldError(fieldId, errors) {
    const input = document.getElementById(fieldId);
    let errorElement = document.getElementById(`${fieldId}-error`);
    
    // Erstelle Error-Element falls nicht vorhanden
    if (! errorElement) {
        errorElement = document.createElement('div');
        errorElement.id = `${fieldId}-error`;
        errorElement.className = 'error-message';
        
        if (input && input.parentElement) {
            input.parentElement.appendChild(errorElement);
        }
    }
    
    if (errors.length > 0) {
        // Zeige ersten Fehler
        if (input) {
            input.classList.add('error');
        }
        errorElement.textContent = errors[0];
        errorElement.classList.add('visible');
        return false;
    } else {
        // Keine Fehler - verstecke Fehlermeldung
        if (input) {
            input. classList.remove('error');
        }
        errorElement.classList. remove('visible');
        return true;
    }
}

/**
 * Validiert alle sichtbaren Felder in der aktuellen Sektion
 * @returns {boolean} - True wenn alle Felder valide
 */
function validateCurrentSection() {
    const section = APP_DATA.sections[APP_STATE.currentSectionIndex];
    let allValid = true;
    
    if (! section || !section.questions) return true;
    
    section.questions.forEach(question => {
        // Überspringe ausgeblendete Fragen
        if (! checkCondition(question)) {
            return;
        }
        
        const value = APP_STATE.answers[question.id];
        const errors = validateField(question, value);
        
        if (! showFieldError(question.id, errors)) {
            allValid = false;
        }
    });
    
    return allValid;
}

// =================================================================
// NEUE INPUT-TYPEN
// =================================================================

/**
 * Erweiterte createStandardInput Funktion mit neuen Typen
 * (Ersetzt die vorhandene in Teil 2/3)
 */
function createStandardInput(question) {
    let input;
    const currentAnswer = APP_STATE.answers[question.id];
    const container = document.createElement('div');
    container.className = 'input-container';

    switch (question.type) {
        case 'text':
        case 'number':
        case 'email': 
        case 'tel':
            input = document.createElement('input');
            input.type = question. type;
            input.value = currentAnswer || '';
            input.id = question.id;
            input.name = question.id;
            input.required = question.required;
            
            // Echtzeit-Validierung
            input. addEventListener('blur', () => {
                const errors = validateField(question, input. value);
                showFieldError(question.id, errors);
            });
            
            input.addEventListener('input', () => {
                handleAnswerChange(input. id, input.value);
                // Clear error on input
                input.classList.remove('error');
                const errorElement = document.getElementById(`${question.id}-error`);
                if (errorElement) {
                    errorElement.classList.remove('visible');
                }
            });
            
            container.appendChild(input);
            break;
            
        case 'date':
            input = document.createElement('input');
            input.type = 'date';
            input.value = currentAnswer || '';
            input. id = question.id;
            input.name = question.id;
            input.required = question. required;
            
            input.addEventListener('change', () => {
                handleAnswerChange(input.id, input.value);
            });
            
            container.appendChild(input);
            break;
            
        case 'time': 
            input = document.createElement('input');
            input.type = 'time';
            input. value = currentAnswer || '';
            input.id = question.id;
            input.name = question. id;
            input.required = question.required;
            
            input.addEventListener('change', () => {
                handleAnswerChange(input.id, input.value);
            });
            
            container.appendChild(input);
            break;
            
        case 'textarea':
            input = document.createElement('textarea');
            input.value = currentAnswer || '';
            input.id = question.id;
            input.name = question.id;
            input.required = question.required;
            input.rows = 4;
            
            input.addEventListener('input', () => {
                handleAnswerChange(input.id, input.value);
            });
            
            container.appendChild(input);
            break;
            
        case 'select':
            input = document.createElement('select');
            input.id = question.id;
            input.name = question.id;
            input.required = question.required;
            
            const defaultOption = document.createElement('option');
            defaultOption.value = '';
            defaultOption.textContent = getTranslation('select_placeholder');
            input.appendChild(defaultOption);

            question.options.forEach(opt => {
                const option = document.createElement('option');
                option.value = opt. value;
                option.textContent = getTranslation(opt.label_key || opt.value);
                if (currentAnswer === opt.value) {
                    option.selected = true;
                }
                input.appendChild(option);
            });
            
            input.addEventListener('change', () => {
                handleAnswerChange(input.id, input.value);
                const errors = validateField(question, input. value);
                showFieldError(question.id, errors);
                renderCurrentSection(); // Re-render für bedingte Fragen
            });
            
            container.appendChild(input);
            break;
            
        case 'multiselect':
            input = document.createElement('div');
            input.className = 'options-list';
            input.id = question.id;
            
            const selectedValues = Array.isArray(currentAnswer) ? currentAnswer : [];

            question.options.forEach(opt => {
                const item = document.createElement('div');
                item.className = 'option-item';
                if (selectedValues.includes(opt. value)) {
                    item. classList.add('selected');
                }
                
                const checkbox = document.createElement('input');
                checkbox.type = 'checkbox';
                checkbox.id = `${question.id}-${opt.value}`;
                checkbox.value = opt.value;
                checkbox.checked = selectedValues.includes(opt. value);
                
                const label = document.createElement('span');
                label.textContent = getTranslation(opt.label_key || opt.value);
                
                item.appendChild(checkbox);
                item.appendChild(label);
                
                item.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
                    if (e.target.tagName !== 'INPUT') {
                        checkbox.checked = !checkbox.checked;
                    }
                    item.classList.toggle('selected', checkbox.checked);
                    
                    let newValues = Array.from(input.querySelectorAll('input:checked')).map(cb => cb.value);
                    handleAnswerChange(question.id, newValues);
                    renderCurrentSection(); // Re-render für bedingte Fragen
                });
                
                input.appendChild(item);
            });
            
            container.appendChild(input);
            return container; // Kein error-element für multiselect
            
        case 'checkbox_freitext':
            const wrapper = document.createElement('div');
            wrapper.className = 'checkbox-freitext-wrapper';
            
            // Checkboxen
            const checkboxDiv = document.createElement('div');
            checkboxDiv.className = 'options-list';
            
            const selectedCheckboxes = Array.isArray(currentAnswer) ? 
                currentAnswer.filter(v => ! v.startsWith('freitext: ')) : [];
            
            question.options.forEach(opt => {
                const item = document.createElement('div');
                item.className = 'option-item';
                if (selectedCheckboxes.includes(opt.value)) {
                    item.classList.add('selected');
                }
                
                const checkbox = document.createElement('input');
                checkbox.type = 'checkbox';
                checkbox.id = `${question.id}-${opt.value}`;
                checkbox.value = opt.value;
                checkbox.checked = selectedCheckboxes.includes(opt.value);
                
                const label = document. createElement('span');
                label. textContent = getTranslation(opt.label_key || opt. value);
                
                item. appendChild(checkbox);
                item. appendChild(label);
                
                item.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
                    if (e.target.tagName !== 'INPUT') {
                        checkbox.checked = !checkbox.checked;
                    }
                    item.classList.toggle('selected', checkbox.checked);
                    updateCheckboxFreitextAnswer();
                });
                
                checkboxDiv.appendChild(item);
            });
            
            wrapper. appendChild(checkboxDiv);
            
            // Freitext-Feld
            const freitextLabel = document.createElement('label');
            freitextLabel.textContent = getTranslation(question.freitext_label || 'additional_notes');
            freitextLabel. style.marginTop = '15px';
            freitextLabel.style.display = 'block';
            freitextLabel.style.fontWeight = '500';
            
            const freitextInput = document.createElement('input');
            freitextInput. type = 'text';
            freitextInput.id = `${question.id}-freitext`;
            freitextInput.placeholder = getTranslation(question.freitext_label || 'additional_notes');
            freitextInput.style. width = '100%';
            freitextInput.style.marginTop = '5px';
            
            // Restore freitext value
            const freitextValue = Array.isArray(currentAnswer) ? 
                currentAnswer.find(v => typeof v === 'string' && v.startsWith('freitext:')) : null;
            if (freitextValue) {
                freitextInput.value = freitextValue. replace('freitext:', '');
            }
            
            freitextInput.addEventListener('input', updateCheckboxFreitextAnswer);
            
            function updateCheckboxFreitextAnswer() {
                let newValues = Array.from(checkboxDiv.querySelectorAll('input:checked')).map(cb => cb.value);
                if (freitextInput.value. trim()) {
                    newValues. push('freitext:' + freitextInput.value.trim());
                }
                handleAnswerChange(question.id, newValues);
            }
            
            wrapper.appendChild(freitextLabel);
            wrapper.appendChild(freitextInput);
            
            return wrapper;
            
        case 'rating':
            const ratingWrapper = document.createElement('div');
            ratingWrapper.className = 'rating-stars';
            ratingWrapper.id = question.id;
            
            for (let i = 1; i <= 5; i++) {
                const star = document.createElement('span');
                star.textContent = '★';
                star.className = 'star';
                star. dataset.value = i;
                
                if (currentAnswer && i <= currentAnswer) {
                    star.classList. add('selected');
                }
                
                star.addEventListener('click', () => {
                    handleAnswerChange(question.id, i);
                    ratingWrapper.querySelectorAll('.star').forEach((s, idx) => {
                        s.classList.toggle('selected', idx < i);
                    });
                });
                
                ratingWrapper. appendChild(star);
            }
            
            return ratingWrapper;
            
        case 'multiple_text':
            const multiWrapper = document.createElement('div');
            multiWrapper.className = 'multiple-text-wrapper';
            multiWrapper.id = question.id;
            
            const values = Array.isArray(currentAnswer) && currentAnswer.length > 0 ? currentAnswer : [''];
            
            function renderInputs() {
                multiWrapper.innerHTML = '';
                
                values.forEach((val, idx) => {
                    const row = document.createElement('div');
                    row.style.marginBottom = '10px';
                    row.style.display = 'flex';
                    row.style. gap = '10px';
                    
                    const inp = document.createElement('input');
                    inp.type = 'text';
                    inp.value = val;
                    inp. placeholder = getTranslation(question. placeholder_key || question.id) + ` ${idx + 1}`;
                    inp.style.flex = '1';
                    
                    inp.addEventListener('input', () => {
                        values[idx] = inp.value;
                        const filteredValues = values.filter(v => v. trim() !== '');
                        handleAnswerChange(question.id, filteredValues. length > 0 ? filteredValues : []);
                    });
                    
                    // Remove button (nur wenn mehr als 1 Feld)
                    if (values.length > 1) {
                        const removeBtn = document. createElement('button');
                        removeBtn.type = 'button';
                        removeBtn.textContent = '✕';
                        removeBtn. className = 'btn-remove';
                        removeBtn.style.padding = '8px 12px';
                        removeBtn. style.backgroundColor = '#ef4444';
                        removeBtn.style.color = 'white';
                        removeBtn.style.border = 'none';
                        removeBtn.style.borderRadius = '4px';
                        removeBtn.style.cursor = 'pointer';
                        
                        removeBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
                            values.splice(idx, 1);
                            renderInputs();
                        });
                        
                        row.appendChild(inp);
                        row.appendChild(removeBtn);
                    } else {
                        row.appendChild(inp);
                    }
                    
                    multiWrapper. appendChild(row);
                });
                
                // Add-Button
                const addBtn = document. createElement('button');
                addBtn.type = 'button';
                addBtn.textContent = '+ ' + getTranslation('add_entry');
                addBtn.className = 'btn-secondary';
                addBtn.style. marginTop = '10px';
                
                addBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
                    values.push('');
                    renderInputs();
                });
                
                multiWrapper.appendChild(addBtn);
            }
            
            renderInputs();
            return multiWrapper;
            
        default:
            input = document.createElement('input');
            input.type = 'text';
            input.value = currentAnswer || '';
            input.id = question.id;
            input.name = question.id;
            input.required = question.required;
            
            input.addEventListener('input', () => {
                handleAnswerChange(input.id, input.value);
            });
            
            container. appendChild(input);
    }
    
    // Error-Element hinzufügen (außer für multiselect, rating, checkbox_freitext, multiple_text)
    if (!['multiselect', 'rating', 'checkbox_freitext', 'multiple_text'].includes(question.type)) {
        const errorMsg = document.createElement('div');
        errorMsg.className = 'error-message';
        errorMsg.id = `${question.id}-error`;
        container.appendChild(errorMsg);
    }
    
    return container;
}

// =================================================================
// NAVIGATION-FUNKTIONEN (Section Skipping)
// =================================================================

/**
 * Findet die nächste sichtbare Sektion
 * @param {number} currentIndex - Aktueller Sektions-Index
 * @returns {number} - Index der nächsten sichtbaren Sektion oder -1
 */
function getNextVisibleSection(currentIndex) {
    for (let i = currentIndex + 1; i < APP_DATA. sections.length; i++) {
        const section = APP_DATA. sections[i];
        
        // Prüfe Section-Bedingung
        if (checkCondition(section)) {
            return i;
        }
    }
    return -1; // Keine weitere Sektion
}

/**
 * Findet die vorherige sichtbare Sektion
 * @param {number} currentIndex - Aktueller Sektions-Index
 * @returns {number} - Index der vorherigen sichtbaren Sektion
 */
function getPreviousVisibleSection(currentIndex) {
    for (let i = currentIndex - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
        const section = APP_DATA.sections[i];
        
        // Prüfe Section-Bedingung
        if (checkCondition(section)) {
            return i;
        }
    }
    return 0; // Erste Sektion
}

// =================================================================
// RESTART-FUNKTIONALITÄT
// =================================================================

/**
 * Kompletter Neustart - löscht alle gespeicherten Daten
 */
function restartApplication() {
    const confirmRestart = confirm(
        getTranslation('restart_confirmation') ||
        'ACHTUNG: Alle gespeicherten Daten werden gelöscht!\n\n' +
        'Möchten Sie wirklich neu starten?'
    );
    
    if (confirmRestart) {
        // Lösche alle gespeicherten Daten
        localStorage.removeItem('anamnese_autosave');
        localStorage.removeItem('encryption_key_hash');
        sessionStorage.removeItem('derived_key');
        
        // Optional: Zweite Bestätigung für Encryption Key
        const deleteKey = confirm(
            getTranslation('restart_delete_key') ||
            'Möchten Sie auch den Verschlüsselungsschlüssel löschen?\n\n' +
            '(Falls Nein, können Sie gespeicherte verschlüsselte Daten später noch laden)'
        );
        
        if (deleteKey) {
            localStorage.removeItem('encryption_key_hash');
        }
        
        // Seite neu laden
        location.reload();
    }
}

// =================================================================
// HILFSFUNKTION:  SANITIZE INPUT
// =================================================================

/**
 * Bereinigt User-Input zur XSS-Prävention
 * @param {string|any} input - Der zu bereinigende Input
 * @returns {string|any} - Bereinigter Input
 */
function sanitizeInput(input) {
    if (typeof input === 'string') {
        return input
            .replace(/</g, '&lt;')
            .replace(/>/g, '&gt;')
            .replace(/"/g, '&quot;')
            .replace(/'/g, '&#x27;')
            .replace(/\//g, '&#x2F;');
    }
    return input;
}

/**
 * Aktualisierte handleAnswerChange mit Sanitization
 */
function handleAnswerChange(id, value) {
    // Sanitize input to prevent XSS
    const sanitizedValue = Array.isArray(value) 
        ? value.map(sanitizeInput)
        : sanitizeInput(value);
    
    // Entferne die Antwort, wenn sie leer ist
    if (sanitizedValue === '' || (Array.isArray(sanitizedValue) && sanitizedValue.length === 0)) {
        delete APP_STATE.answers[id];
    } else {
        APP_STATE.answers[id] = sanitizedValue;
    }
    
    // Schedule auto-save after changes
    scheduleAutoSave();
}

// =================================================================
// ÜBERSETZUNGEN FÜR VALIDIERUNG & NEUE FUNKTIONEN
// =================================================================
```

```html
<script>
// =================================================================
// RENDERING-FUNKTIONEN (FINAL)
// =================================================================

/**
 * Rendert die aktuelle Sektion mit allen Fragen
 */
function renderCurrentSection() {
    const section = APP_DATA.sections[APP_STATE.currentSectionIndex];
    const formContainer = document.getElementById('form-container');
    
    if (!formContainer || !section) return;
    
    formContainer.innerHTML = '';

    // Titel der Sektion
    const title = document.createElement('h2');
    title.textContent = getTranslation(section.id);
    title.style.marginBottom = '30px';
    formContainer.appendChild(title);

    // Fragen rendern
    section.questions.forEach(question => {
        const questionElement = document.createElement('div');
        questionElement.className = 'form-group';
        questionElement.id = `question-${question.id}`;
        
        // Bedingung prüfen
        const isVisible = checkCondition(question);
        
        if (! isVisible) {
            questionElement.style.display = 'none';
            delete APP_STATE.answers[question.id];
            return;
        }

        questionElement.style.display = 'block';

        // Label
        const label = document.createElement('label');
        label.className = 'question-label';
        label.innerHTML = getTranslation('label_' + question.id) + 
                         (question.required ? ' <span class="required-star">*</span>' : '');
        questionElement.appendChild(label);

        // Input-Element erstellen
        let inputElement;
        
        if (question.id. startsWith('0003_')) {
            inputElement = createDateSelect(question);
        } else {
            inputElement = createStandardInput(question);
        }

        questionElement.appendChild(inputElement);
        formContainer.appendChild(questionElement);
    });
    
    updateNavigationButtons();
}

/**
 * Aktualisiert Navigation-Buttons
 */
function updateNavigationButtons() {
    const prevBtn = document.getElementById('prev-btn');
    const nextBtn = document.getElementById('next-btn');
    
    if (prevBtn) {
        prevBtn.disabled = APP_STATE.currentSectionIndex === 0;
    }
    
    if (nextBtn) {
        const isLastSection = getNextVisibleSection(APP_STATE.currentSectionIndex) === -1;
        nextBtn.textContent = isLastSection ? 
            getTranslation('btn_export') || 'Export & Finish' : 
            getTranslation('btn_next') || 'Next →';
    }
}

/**
 * Aktualisiert Progress Bar
 */
function updateProgress() {
    const totalSections = APP_DATA.sections.length;
    const currentSection = APP_STATE.currentSectionIndex + 1;
    const progress = (currentSection / totalSections) * 100;
    
    const progressFill = document.getElementById('progress-fill');
    const progressText = document.getElementById('progress-text');
    
    if (progressFill) {
        progressFill.style.width = `${Math.min(progress, 100)}%`;
    }
    
    if (progressText) {
        progressText. textContent = `${getTranslation('section')} ${currentSection} ${getTranslation('of')} ${totalSections}`;
    }
}

/**
 * Übersetzungsfunktion mit Fallback
 */
function getTranslation(key) {
    const lang = APP_STATE.currentLanguage || 'en';
    
    if (! TRANSLATIONS[lang]) {
        console.warn(`Language ${lang} not found, falling back to English`);
        return TRANSLATIONS.en[key] || key;
    }
    
    return TRANSLATIONS[lang][key] || TRANSLATIONS.en[key] || key;
}

// =================================================================
// APPLICATION CONTROLLER
// =================================================================

const App = {
    /**
     * Initialisiert die Anwendung
     */
    init:  async function() {
        try {
            console.log('Initializing Medical History Questionnaire v8.. .');
            
            // Setup encryption
            await setupEncryptionKey();
            
            // Restore auto-save if available
            const restored = restoreAutoSave();
            
            if (restored) {
                console. log('Auto-save restored');
            }
            
            // Initialize OCR
            initOCRUpload();
            
            // Update UI language
            this.updateUILanguage();
            
            // Render first section
            renderCurrentSection();
            updateProgress();
            
            console.log('Application initialized successfully');
            
        } catch (e) {
            console.error('Initialization error:', e);
            alert(getTranslation('init_error') || 'Failed to initialize application:  ' + e.message);
        }
    },
    
    /**
     * Wechselt die Sprache
     */
    changeLanguage: function(lang) {
        APP_STATE. currentLanguage = lang;
        
        // Update active language button
        document.querySelectorAll('.language-switcher button').forEach(btn => {
            btn.classList.toggle('active', btn.dataset.lang === lang);
        });
        
        // Update HTML lang attribute
        document.documentElement. lang = lang;
        
        // Update UI
        this.updateUILanguage();
        renderCurrentSection();
        updateProgress();
        
        // Save preference
        localStorage.setItem('preferred_language', lang);
    },
    
    /**
     * Aktualisiert UI-Texte
     */
    updateUILanguage: function() {
        const elements = {
            'app-title': getTranslation('app_title'),
            'app-subtitle': getTranslation('app_subtitle'),
            'upload-title': getTranslation('upload_title'),
            'upload-subtitle': getTranslation('upload_subtitle'),
            'next-btn': getTranslation('btn_next'),
            'prev-btn': getTranslation('btn_previous')
        };
        
        Object.entries(elements).forEach(([id, text]) => {
            const el = document.getElementById(id);
            if (el) {
                el.textContent = text;
            }
        });
    },
    
    /**
     * Geht zur nächsten Sektion
     */
    nextSection:  function() {
        // Validate current section
        if (! validateCurrentSection()) {
            alert(getTranslation('validation_required'));
            return;
        }
        
        const nextIndex = getNextVisibleSection(APP_STATE.currentSectionIndex);
        
        if (nextIndex === -1) {
            // Letzter Schritt - Export
            this.exportData();
        } else {
            APP_STATE.currentSectionIndex = nextIndex;
            renderCurrentSection();
            updateProgress();
            window.scrollTo(0, 0);
        }
    },
    
    /**
     * Geht zur vorherigen Sektion
     */
    previousSection: function() {
        const prevIndex = getPreviousVisibleSection(APP_STATE.currentSectionIndex);
        APP_STATE.currentSectionIndex = prevIndex;
        renderCurrentSection();
        updateProgress();
        window.scrollTo(0, 0);
    },
    
    /**
     * Exportiert die Daten verschlüsselt
     */
    exportData: async function() {
        const answerJson = {
            metadata: {
                version: APP_DATA.version,
                timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
                language: APP_STATE.currentLanguage,
                app_title: getTranslation('app_title')
            },
            answers: APP_STATE.answers
        };
        
        const jsonString = JSON.stringify(answerJson, null, 2);
        
        try {
            const encryptedData = await encryptData(jsonString);
            
            // Create download
            const blob = new Blob([encryptedData], { type:  'text/plain' });
            const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
            const a = document. createElement('a');
            a.href = url;
            
            // Filename with timestamp
            const timestamp = new Date().toISOString().replace(/[:.]/g, '-').slice(0, -5);
            a.download = `anamnese_${timestamp}_encrypted.txt`;
            
            document.body.appendChild(a);
            a.click();
            document.body.removeChild(a);
            URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
            
            // Clear auto-save after successful export
            localStorage.removeItem('anamnese_autosave');
            
            alert(getTranslation('export_success') || '✅ Data exported successfully!\n\nPlease send this file to your healthcare provider.');
            
        } catch (e) {
            console.error('Export error:', e);
            alert(getTranslation('export_error') || 'Export failed: ' + e.message);
        }
    }
};

// Zusätzliche Übersetzungen für App Controller
TRANSLATIONS.de = {
    ...TRANSLATIONS.de,
    section: 'Abschnitt',
    of: 'von',
    init_error: 'Fehler beim Initialisieren der Anwendung: ',
    export_success: '✅ Daten erfolgreich exportiert!\n\nBitte senden Sie diese Datei an Ihren Arzt.',
    export_error: 'Export fehlgeschlagen:'
};

TRANSLATIONS.en = {

    of: 'of',

    export_error: 'Export failed:'
};

TRANSLATIONS.fr = {

    export_success: '✅ Données exportées avec succès!\n\nVeuillez envoyer ce fichier à votre médecin.',
    export_error: "L'exportation a échoué:"
};

// =================================================================

// Initialize on DOM ready
window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    // Check for saved language preference
    const savedLang = localStorage.getItem('preferred_language');
    if (savedLang && TRANSLATIONS[savedLang]) {
        APP_STATE.currentLanguage = savedLang;
    } else {
        // Default to English
        APP_STATE.currentLanguage = 'en';
    }
    
    // Initialize app
    App.init();
});

// Prevent accidental page leave
window.addEventListener('beforeunload', (e) => {
    // Check if there are unsaved answers
    if (Object.keys(APP_STATE.answers).length > 0) {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.returnValue = '';
        return '';
    }
});

</script>
</head>
```

```javascript
// Aktuell:  "Section 5 of 34" (verwirrend bei übersprungenen Sektionen)
// Besser: "Step 3 of 8 visible sections"

function updateProgress() {
    const visibleSections = APP_DATA.sections.filter(s => checkCondition(s));
    const currentVisibleIndex = visibleSections. findIndex(s => 
        s === APP_DATA.sections[APP_STATE.currentSectionIndex]
    ) + 1;
    
    const progress = (currentVisibleIndex / visibleSections.length) * 100;
    document.getElementById('progress-fill').style.width = `${progress}%`;
    document.getElementById('progress-text').textContent = 
        `${getTranslation('step')} ${currentVisibleIndex} ${getTranslation('of')} ${visibleSections.length}`;
}
```

## **6. 🔐 SICHERHEITS-VERBESSERUNGEN**

### **A) Content Security Policy verschärfen**
```html
<meta http-equiv="Content-Security-Policy" 
      content="default-src 'self'; 
               script-src 'self' 'sha256-HASH-OF-INLINE-SCRIPT' https://cdn.jsdelivr.net; 
               style-src 'self' 'sha256-HASH-OF-INLINE-STYLE';
               img-src 'self' data:  blob:;
               connect-src 'self';
               form-action 'none';
               base-uri 'self';
               frame-ancestors 'none';">
```

### **B) Verschlüsselung mit Passwort-Stärke-Meter**
```javascript
function checkPasswordStrength(password) {
    let strength = 0;
    if (password.length >= 16) strength++;
    if (/[a-z]/.test(password) && /[A-Z]/. test(password)) strength++;
    if (/[0-9]/.test(password)) strength++;
    if (/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/.test(password)) strength++;
    
    return ['very weak', 'weak', 'medium', 'strong', 'very strong'][strength];
}
```

### **C) Rate Limiting für Passwort-Eingabe**
```javascript
let loginAttempts = 0;
let lockoutTime = null;

async function setupEncryptionKey(retryCount = 0) {
    // Prüfe Lockout
    if (lockoutTime && Date.now() < lockoutTime) {
        const remainingSeconds = Math.ceil((lockoutTime - Date.now()) / 1000);
        alert(`Too many attempts. Please wait ${remainingSeconds} seconds. `);
        return;
    }
    
    // Nach 3 Versuchen:  30 Sekunden Lockout
    if (loginAttempts >= 3) {
        lockoutTime = Date.now() + 30000;
        loginAttempts = 0;
        return setupEncryptionKey(0);
    }
    
    // ...  rest of function
    loginAttempts++;
}
```

---

## **7. 💾 DATEN-PERSISTENZ VERBESSERN**

### **A) IndexedDB statt localStorage**
```javascript
// localStorage Limit: ~5-10 MB
// IndexedDB:  praktisch unbegrenzt

class Storage {
    async init() {
        return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
            const request = indexedDB.open('AnamneseDB', 1);
            request.onsuccess = () => {
                this.db = request. result;
                resolve();
            };
            request.onupgradeneeded = (e) => {
                const db = e.target.result;
                db.createObjectStore('answers', { keyPath: 'id' });
            };
        });
    }
    
    async saveAnswers(answers) {
        const tx = this.db.transaction('answers', 'readwrite');
        await tx.objectStore('answers').put({ 
            id: 'current', 
            data: answers,
            timestamp: Date.now() 
        });
    }
}
```

### **B) Versionierung für Wiederherstellung**
```javascript
// Speichere mehrere Versionen
function saveVersion() {
    const versions = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('anamnese_versions') || '[]');
    versions.push({
        timestamp: Date.now(),
        answers: APP_STATE.answers,
        section: APP_STATE.currentSectionIndex
    });
    
    // Behalte nur letzte 5 Versionen
    if (versions.length > 5) versions.shift();
    
    localStorage.setItem('anamnese_versions', JSON.stringify(versions));
}
```

### **B) Unit Tests**
```javascript
// Test-Suite einbauen
function runTests() {
    console.group('Running Tests.. .');
    
    // Test 1: Age Calculation
    APP_STATE.answers['0003_jahr'] = '1990';
    console.assert(calculateAge() === 34, 'Age calculation failed');
    
    // Test 2: Condition Check
    console.assert(checkSingleCondition({
        field: 'age',
        value: 30,
        operator: '>'
    }) === true, 'Age condition failed');
    
    // Test 3: Validation
    const errors = validateField({
        id: 'test',
        required: true,
        validation: { minLength: 3 }
    }, 'ab');
    console.assert(errors. length > 0, 'Validation failed');
    
    console.groupEnd();
}

// Auto-run in Debug-Mode
if (DEBUG_MODE) runTests();
```

## **9. 📊 ANALYTICS & TELEMETRY (Optional)**

### **GDPR-konform, lokal:**
```javascript
const Analytics = {
    events: [],
    
    track(event, data) {
        this.events.push({
            event,
            data,
            timestamp:  Date.now()
        });
        
        // Speichere lokal (nicht senden!)
        localStorage.setItem('analytics', JSON.stringify(this.events));
    },
    
    // Beispiele:
    trackSectionTime(sectionId, timeSpent) {
        this.track('section_completed', { sectionId, timeSpent });
    },
    
    trackError(error) {
        this.track('error', { message: error.message, stack: error.stack });
    },
    
    getReport() {
        return {
            totalTime: this.events.reduce((sum, e) => sum + (e.data.timeSpent || 0), 0),
            completionRate: APP_STATE.currentSectionIndex / APP_DATA.sections.length,
            errors: this.events.filter(e => e.event === 'error')
        };
    }
};
```

## **10. 🎯 PERFORMANCE-OPTIMIERUNG**

### **A) Lazy Loading für Sektionen**
```javascript
// Lade nur aktuelle + nächste Sektion
function renderCurrentSection() {
    // Aktuell:  Alle Sektionen werden immer geprüft
    // Besser: Nur sichtbare Sektionen laden
    
    const visibleSections = [
        APP_STATE.currentSectionIndex - 1,
        APP_STATE.currentSectionIndex,
        APP_STATE.currentSectionIndex + 1
    ].filter(i => i >= 0 && i < APP_DATA.sections.length);
    
    // Nur diese Sektionen rendern
}
```

### **B) Debouncing für Auto-Save**
```javascript
// Aktuell: Auto-Save nach jedem Input
// Besser: Nur bei Inaktivität
let saveTimeout;
function scheduleAutoSave() {
    clearTimeout(saveTimeout);
    saveTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
        saveToLocalStorage();
    }, 2000); // Erst nach 2 Sekunden Pause
}
```

### **C) Virtual Scrolling für große Listen**
```javascript
// Bei vielen Optionen (> 50)
// Nur sichtbare Elemente rendern
```

---

## **11. 🔄 DATEN-IMPORT/-EXPORT ERWEITERN**

### **A) Mehrere Export-Formate**
```javascript
exportData(format = 'encrypted') {
    switch(format) {
        case 'encrypted':
            return this.exportEncrypted();
        case 'json':
            return this. exportJSON();
        case 'pdf':
            return this.exportPDF();
        case 'fhir':
            return this. exportFHIR(); // HL7 FHIR Format
        case 'hl7':
            return this. exportHL7();
    }
}
```

### **B) Import-Funktionalität**
```javascript
// Lade vorherige Daten
function importData(file) {
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = async (e) => {
        const decrypted = await decryptData(e.target.result);
        const data = JSON.parse(decrypted);
        APP_STATE.answers = data.answers;
        renderCurrentSection();
    };
    reader.readAsText(file);
}
```

```json
    },
    {
      "src":  "icon-512.png",

      "type": "image/png"
    }
  ]
}
```

---

**Status:** 📋 Teil 1.3/12 der Label-Liste komplett

**Was ist enthalten:**
- ✅ Neurologische Beschwerden (1080-1189) - 26 Labels
- ✅ Urologische/Gynäkologische Beschwerden (1090-1194) - 38 Labels
- ✅ Schwangerschaft (1290-1390) - 20 Labels
- ✅ Augenbeschwerden (1A00) - 15 Labels
- ✅ HNO-Beschwerden (1B00-1B06) - 40 Labels
- ✅ Psychische Beschwerden (1C00-1C15) - 16 Labels
- ✅ Pädiatrische Fragen (1P00-1P40) - 24 Labels

**GESAMT in Teil 1.3:** ~179 Labels

**GESAMT bisher (1.1 + 1.2 + 1.3):** ~450 Labels

**Nächster Teil 1.4 wird enthalten:**
- Terminvereinbarung (2000-2100)
- Kontrolluntersuchung, Vorsorge, Befunde
- Chronische Erkrankungen Details
- Unfalldetails
- Begutachtung

**Soll ich mit Teil 1.4 fortfahren?** 🚀

- ✅ MRSA (7007) - 3 Labels
- ✅ Nierenerkrankungen (7008) - 6 Labels
- ✅ Nervenerkrankungen (7009) - 8 Labels
- ✅ Rheuma (7010) - 7 Labels
- ✅ Schilddrüse (7011) - 8 Labels

**GESAMT in Teil 1.5:** ~214 Labels

**GESAMT bisher (1.1 + 1.2 + 1.3 + 1.4 + 1.5):** ~848 Labels

**Nächster Teil 1.6 wird enthalten:**
- Vorerkrankungen & Operationen (8000-8016)
- Geschlechts-spezifische Vorsorge (8501-8504, 8800)
- Medikamente (8900)
- Abschluss (9000, 9001, 9900)

**Soll ich mit Teil 1.6 (FINAL der Label-Liste) fortfahren?** 🚀

```javascript
// BEISPIELE FEHLENDER LABELS:

label_2042_andere_freitext: "Welche Gefäßerkrankung?",

// Schwangerschaft - fehlende Labels

```

## **✅ LÖSUNG:  ERWEITERTE LABEL-LISTE TEIL 1.7**

**Soll ich jetzt TEIL 1.7 erstellen mit allen fehlenden Labels?**

Das würde umfassen:
- ✅ Datenschutz & DSGVO (30+ Labels)
- ✅ Fehlende Fragen-Labels (50+ Labels)
- ✅ UI Actions & Buttons (30+ Labels)
- ✅ Auto-Save Meldungen (10+ Labels)
- ✅ Export Dialog (15+ Labels)
- ✅ Erweiterte Fehlermeldungen (20+ Labels)
- ✅ Mobile-Hinweise (10+ Labels)
- ✅ Hilfe-Texte (15+ Labels)
- ✅ Placeholders (50+ Labels)
- ✅ Progress-Anzeige (10+ Labels)
- ✅ Restart/Reset (10+ Labels)
- ✅ Sprach-Wechsel (20+ Labels)
- ✅ Passwort/Verschlüsselung (25+ Labels)

**GESAMT: ~300 zusätzliche Labels**

**Neue Gesamtsumme: ~1250 Labels für vollständige Übersetzung**

---

**Bestätigen Sie:**
- **"JA - Teil 1.7 erstellen"** = Ich erstelle die fehlenden 300 Labels
- **"DIREKT ZU ÜBERSETZUNGEN"** = Wir beginnen mit Übersetzungen und fügen fehlende Labels später hinzu

**Was möchten Sie? ** 🚀
